    <script>
    function initAll() {
        const glow = document.getElementById("cursor-glow");
        const dot = document.getElementById("cursor-dot");

        const moveCursor = (e) => {
            if (glow && dot) {
                glow.style.left = e.clientX + "px";
                glow.style.top = e.clientY + "px";
                dot.style.left = e.clientX + "px";
                dot.style.top = e.clientY + "px";
            }
        };
        
        document.removeEventListener("mousemove", moveCursor);
        document.addEventListener("mousemove", moveCursor);

        const storedName = localStorage.getItem('userName');
        const greetingElement = document.getElementById("user-greeting");
        if (storedName && greetingElement) {
            const cleanName = storedName.trim().split(' ')[0];
            const capitalized = cleanName.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + cleanName.slice(1);
            greetingElement.innerText = `Welcome, ${capitalized}`;
        } else if (greetingElement) {
            greetingElement.innerText = `Welcome!`;
        }

        document.onmousedown = () => {
            if(dot) dot.style.transform = "translate(-50%, -50%) scale(1.5)";
        };
        document.onmouseup = () => {
            if(dot) dot.style.transform = "translate(-50%, -50%) scale(1)";
        };
    }

    async function analyzeResume() {
      const job = document.getElementById("dream-job").value;
      const btn = document.getElementById("ai-analyze-btn");
      const resultArea = document.getElementById("ai-result-area");
      
      const scoreNumber = document.getElementById("ai-score-number");
      const scoreRing = document.getElementById("ai-score-ring");
      const atsNumber = document.getElementById("ai-ats-number");
      const atsRing = document.getElementById("ai-ats-ring");
      
      const suggestionsDiv = document.getElementById("ai-suggestions");

      if (!job) return alert("Please enter your dream job!");

      btn.innerText = "Analyzing...";
      btn.disabled = true;

      try {
          const resumeText = document.getElementById("preview").innerText;

          const response = await fetch("http://localhost:5000/api/ai/analyze", {
              method: "POST",
              headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
              body: JSON.stringify({ jobTitle: job, resumeData: resumeText }),
          });

          if (!response.ok) throw new Error("Server responded with an error");

          const data = await response.json();
          console.log("📥 AI Data:", data);

          if (resultArea) resultArea.style.display = "block";

          const circumference = 377; // Math for 140px size

          // --- 1. JOB MATCH SCORE ---
          const rawScore = parseInt(data.score || data.jobScore || 0);
          if (scoreNumber && scoreRing) {
            scoreNumber.innerText = rawScore;
            const hue = (rawScore / 100) * 120;
            const color = `hsl(${hue}, 85%, 50%)`;

            scoreRing.style.stroke = color;
            scoreNumber.style.color = color;
            scoreNumber.style.textShadow = `0 0 10px ${color}`;

            const offset = circumference - (rawScore / 100) * circumference;
            scoreRing.style.transition = "none";
            scoreRing.style.strokeDashoffset = circumference;
            void scoreRing.offsetWidth;

            setTimeout(() => {
              scoreRing.style.transition = "stroke-dashoffset 1.5s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1), stroke 1.5s ease";
              scoreRing.style.strokeDashoffset = offset;
            }, 50);
          }

          // --- 2. ATS SCORE ---
          const rawAts = parseInt(data.atsScore || data.ats_score || data.ATS || 0);
          if (atsNumber && atsRing) {
            atsNumber.innerText = rawAts;
            const atsHue = (rawAts / 100) * 120;
            const atsColor = `hsl(${atsHue}, 85%, 50%)`;

            atsRing.style.stroke = atsColor;
            atsNumber.style.color = atsColor;
            atsNumber.style.textShadow = `0 0 10px ${atsColor}`;

            const atsOffset = circumference - (rawAts / 100) * circumference;
            atsRing.style.transition = "none";
            atsRing.style.strokeDashoffset = circumference;
            void atsRing.offsetWidth;

            setTimeout(() => {
              atsRing.style.transition = "stroke-dashoffset 1.5s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1), stroke 1.5s ease";
              atsRing.style.strokeDashoffset = atsOffset;
            }, 50);
          }

          // --- 3. SUGGESTIONS ---
          if (suggestionsDiv) {
            if (data.suggestions) {
              suggestionsDiv.innerHTML = data.suggestions
                .replace(/\n/g, "<br>")
                .replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, "<strong>$1</strong>");
            } else {
              suggestionsDiv.innerHTML = "No specific suggestions found.";
            }
          }

          if (resultArea) resultArea.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth" });
      } catch (err) {
          console.error("Audit Error:", err);
          alert("Connection to AI server failed.");
      } finally {
          if (btn) {
              btn.innerText = "Audit";
              btn.disabled = false;
          }
      }
    }

    function toggleTheme() {
        const body = document.body;
        const icon = document.getElementById("theme-icon");
        if (body.getAttribute("data-theme") === "dark") {
            body.removeAttribute("data-theme");
            icon.innerHTML = '<path d="M21 12.79A9 9 0 1 1 11.21 3 7 7 0 0 0 21 12.79z"></path>';
        } else {
            body.setAttribute("data-theme", "dark");
            icon.innerHTML = '<circle cx="12" cy="12" r="5"></circle><line x1="12" y1="1" x2="12" y2="3"></line><line x1="12" y1="21" x2="12" y2="23"></line><line x1="4.22" y1="4.22" x2="5.64" y2="5.64"></line><line x1="18.36" y1="18.36" x2="19.78" y2="19.78"></line><line x1="1" y1="12" x2="3" y2="12"></line><line x1="21" y1="12" x2="23" y2="12"></line><line x1="4.22" y1="19.78" x2="5.64" y2="18.36"></line><line x1="18.36" y1="5.64" x2="19.78" y2="4.22"></line>';
        }
    }

   function downloadResumePDF() {
      const overlay = document.getElementById("print-overlay");
      const preview = document.getElementById("preview");

      // Show the loading overlay
      if (overlay) overlay.classList.add("visible");

      // Remove animation class so no transform is active
      preview.classList.remove("animating");

      // Give the browser one frame to settle, then print
      requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        requestAnimationFrame(() => {
          if (overlay) overlay.classList.remove("visible");

          // Small delay so overlay hide is visually clean before dialog
          setTimeout(() => {
            window.print();
          }, 80);
        });
      });
    }

    function signOut() {
        localStorage.removeItem("userId");
        localStorage.removeItem("token");
        localStorage.removeItem("userName");
        const btn = document.querySelector(".btn-signout");
        if (btn) btn.innerText = "Signing out...";
        setTimeout(() => { window.location.href = "index.html"; }, 500);
    }

    window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
        initAll();
    });

      // 🚨 FIXED: INLINED SVG STYLES TO PREVENT MASSIVE ICONS IN STUDIO 🚨

      function getUrl(url) {
        let u = esc(url).trim();
        if(u && !u.startsWith('http') && !u.startsWith('mailto:')) return 'https://' + u;
        return u;
      }

      function normalizeState() {
        state.education = state.education || [];
        state.experience = state.experience || [];
        state.projects = state.projects || [];
        state.techSkills = state.techSkills || [];
        state.achievements = state.achievements || [];
        state.certifications = state.certifications || [];
        state.extracurricular = state.extracurricular || [];
        state.coursework = state.coursework || "";
        state.skills = state.skills || "";
        state.languages = state.languages || "";
        state.hobbies = state.hobbies || "";
        state.summary = state.summary || "";
        state.refs = state.refs || "";
        state.skillLevels = state.skillLevels || [];
        state.references = state.references || [];
      }

      function esc(str) {
        if (!str) return "";
        return String(str)
          .replace(/&/g, "&amp;")
          .replace(/</g, "&lt;")
          .replace(/>/g, "&gt;")
          .replace(/"/g, "&quot;");
      }

      function formatText(text) {
        if (!text) return "";
        let escaped = esc(text);
        escaped = escaped.replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, "<strong>$1</strong>");
        
        // Match Markdown format [Text](URL)
        // Uses color:inherit so it respects the template's color choice
        escaped = escaped.replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\(([^)]+)\)/g, '<a href="$2" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:inherit; text-decoration:underline; text-underline-offset:2px;">$1</a>');
        
        return escaped;
      }

      function formatDescToLi(desc) {
        if (!desc) return "";
        return desc.split('\n')
          .map(line => line.trim())
          .filter(line => line.length > 0)
          .map(line => {
              // 🚨 FIX: Remove leading bullets or dashes if user types them, prevents double bulleting 🚨
              let cleanedLine = line.replace(/^[•\-]\s*/, '');
              return `<li>${formatText(cleanedLine)}</li>`;
          })
          .join('');
      }

      function triggerPreviewAnimation() {
        const p = document.getElementById("preview");
        p.classList.remove("animating");
        void p.offsetWidth;
        p.classList.add("animating");
      }

      function updateTemplate(val) {
        state.template = val;
        document.querySelectorAll("[data-show]").forEach((el) => {
          const allowed = el.getAttribute("data-show").split(",");
          el.style.display = allowed.includes(state.template)
            ? el.getAttribute("data-display") || "block"
            : "none";
        });
        render();
        triggerPreviewAnimation();
      }

      function update(key, val) {
        state[key] = val;
        render();
      }

      function add(type) {
        normalizeState();
        if (type === "experience")
          state.experience.push({ title: "", company: "", date: "", desc: "" });
        if (type === "education")
          state.education.push({ school: "", degree: "", date: "", location: "" });
        if (type === "projects")
          state.projects.push({ title: "", tech: "", link: "", liveLink: "", desc: "" });
        if (type === "techSkills")
          state.techSkills.push({ cat: "", items: "" });
        if (type === "achievements") state.achievements.push("");
        if (type === "certifications") 
          state.certifications.push({ name: "", date: "", link: ""});
        if (type === "extracurricular")
          state.extracurricular.push({ org: "", role: "", date: "", desc: ""});
        if (type === "skillLevels")
          state.skillLevels.push({ name: "", level: "50" });
        if (type === "references")
          state.references.push({ name: "", role: "", company: "" });
        
        renderInputs();
        render();
      }

      function remove(type, i) {
        state[type].splice(i, 1);
        renderInputs();
        render();
      }

      function clearAll() {
        if (confirm("Are you sure you want to clear all data and start blank?")) {
          state = {
            template: state.template,
            photo: "", name: "", role: "", email: "", phone: "", address: "", linkedin: "", github: "", summary: "", refs: "",
            education: [], experience: [], projects: [], techSkills: [], achievements: [], skills: "", languages: "", hobbies: "", coursework: "", certifications: [], extracurricular: [], skillLevels: [], references: []
          };
          renderInputs();
          render();
        }
      }

      function handleImg(input) {
        if (!input.files[0]) return;
        const reader = new FileReader();
        reader.onload = (e) => {
          state.photo = e.target.result;
          render();
        };
        reader.readAsDataURL(input.files[0]);
      }

      function renderInputs() {
        normalizeState();

        document.getElementById("in-name").value = state.name;
        document.getElementById("in-role").value = state.role;
        document.getElementById("in-phone").value = state.phone;
        document.getElementById("in-email").value = state.email;
        document.getElementById("in-linkedin").value = state.linkedin;
        document.getElementById("in-github").value = state.github;
        document.getElementById("in-address").value = state.address;
        document.getElementById("in-summary").value = state.summary;
        if (document.getElementById("in-refs")) document.getElementById("in-refs").value = state.refs;
        document.getElementById("in-skills").value = state.skills;
        if (document.getElementById("in-languages")) document.getElementById("in-languages").value = state.languages;
        document.getElementById("in-hobbies").value = state.hobbies;
        if (document.getElementById("in-coursework")) document.getElementById("in-coursework").value = state.coursework || '';

        document.getElementById("edu-fields").innerHTML = state.education
          .map((item, i) => `
          <div class="dynamic-item">
            <button class="btn-del" onclick="remove('education', ${i})">×</button>
            <input placeholder="School / College" value="${esc(item.school)}" oninput="state.education[${i}].school=this.value; render()" style="margin-bottom:8px">
            <input placeholder="Degree / Details" value="${esc(item.degree)}" oninput="state.education[${i}].degree=this.value; render()" style="margin-bottom:8px">
            <div class="form-grid"><input placeholder="Dates" value="${esc(item.date)}" oninput="state.education[${i}].date=this.value; render()"><input placeholder="Location" value="${esc(item.location)}" oninput="state.education[${i}].location=this.value; render()"></div>
          </div>`)
          .join("");

        document.getElementById("exp-fields").innerHTML = state.experience
          .map((item, i) => `
          <div class="dynamic-item">
            <button class="btn-del" onclick="remove('experience', ${i})">×</button>
            <input placeholder="Job Title" value="${esc(item.title)}" oninput="state.experience[${i}].title=this.value; isPristine=false; render()" style="margin-bottom:8px">
            <div class="form-grid" style="margin-bottom:8px"><input placeholder="Company" value="${esc(item.company)}" oninput="state.experience[${i}].company=this.value; isPristine=false; render()"><input placeholder="Dates" value="${esc(item.date)}" oninput="state.experience[${i}].date=this.value; isPristine=false; render()"></div>
            <div class="label-row" style="margin-top:8px;"><label style="font-size:10px; color:var(--text-muted);">Description</label><button class="btn-ai" onclick="rewriteText(event, 'experience', ${i})">✨ Enhance</button></div>
            <textarea placeholder="Description (Supports multiline for bullets and **bold** text)" oninput="state.experience[${i}].desc=this.value; isPristine=false; render()">${esc(item.desc)}</textarea>
          </div>`)
          .join("");

       document.getElementById("proj-fields").innerHTML = state.projects
          .map((item, i) => `
          <div class="dynamic-item">
            <button class="btn-del" onclick="remove('projects', ${i})">×</button>
            <div class="form-grid" style="margin-bottom:8px">
              <input placeholder="Project Name" value="${esc(item.title)}" oninput="state.projects[${i}].title=this.value; isPristine=false; render()">
              <input placeholder="Date (e.g. Oct 2023)" value="${esc(item.date || '')}" oninput="state.projects[${i}].date=this.value; isPristine=false; render()">
            </div>
            <input placeholder="Tech Used" value="${esc(item.tech)}" oninput="state.projects[${i}].tech=this.value; isPristine=false; render()" style="margin-bottom:8px">
            <div class="form-grid" style="margin-bottom:8px"><input placeholder="GitHub Link" value="${esc(item.link)}" oninput="state.projects[${i}].link=this.value; isPristine=false; render()"><input placeholder="Live Link (Optional)" value="${esc(item.liveLink || '')}" oninput="state.projects[${i}].liveLink=this.value; isPristine=false; render()"></div>
            <div class="label-row" style="margin-top:8px;"><label style="font-size:10px; color:var(--text-muted);">Description</label><button class="btn-ai" onclick="rewriteText(event, 'projects', ${i})">✨ Enhance</button></div>
            <textarea placeholder="Description (Supports multiline for bullets and **bold** text)" oninput="state.projects[${i}].desc=this.value; isPristine=false; render()">${esc(item.desc)}</textarea>
          </div>`)
          .join("");

        document.getElementById("tech-skill-fields").innerHTML = state.techSkills
          .map((item, i) => `
          <div class="dynamic-item">
            <button class="btn-del" onclick="remove('techSkills', ${i})">×</button>
            <input placeholder="Category (e.g. Languages)" value="${esc(item.cat)}" oninput="state.techSkills[${i}].cat=this.value; render()" style="margin-bottom:8px">
            <input placeholder="Skills (e.g. C, C++, Python)" value="${esc(item.items)}" oninput="state.techSkills[${i}].items=this.value; render()">
          </div>`)
          .join("");

        document.getElementById("achieve-fields").innerHTML = state.achievements
          .map((item, i) => `
          <div class="dynamic-item">
            <button class="btn-del" onclick="remove('achievements', ${i})">×</button>
            <textarea placeholder="${state.template === 'academic' ? 'Detail (Press Enter for new items)' : 'Achievement details (Press Enter for new bullets, use **word** for bold)'}" oninput="state.achievements[${i}]=this.value; render()" style="min-height: 80px; margin:0;">${esc(item)}</textarea>
          </div>`)
          .join("");

        if(document.getElementById("cert-fields")) {
          document.getElementById("cert-fields").innerHTML = state.certifications
            .map((item, i) => `
            <div class="dynamic-item">
              <button class="btn-del" onclick="remove('certifications', ${i})">×</button>
              <div class="form-grid" style="margin-bottom:8px">
                <input placeholder="${state.template === 'attorney' ? 'Hackathon Name (Use ** for bold)' : 'Certification Name'}" value="${esc(item.name)}" oninput="state.certifications[${i}].name=this.value; render()">
                <input placeholder="${state.template === 'attorney' ? 'Rank / Details (Use ** for bold)' : 'Date (e.g. March 2025)'}" value="${esc(item.date)}" oninput="state.certifications[${i}].date=this.value; render()">
              </div>
              <input placeholder="Certificate Link (URL)" value="${esc(item.link || '')}" oninput="state.certifications[${i}].link=this.value; render()">
            </div>`)
            .join("");
        }

       if(document.getElementById("extra-fields")) {
          document.getElementById("extra-fields").innerHTML = state.extracurricular
            .map((item, i) => `
            <div class="dynamic-item">
              <button class="btn-del" onclick="remove('extracurricular', ${i})">×</button>
              <div class="form-grid" style="margin-bottom:8px">
                <input placeholder="${state.template === 'attorney' ? 'Position & Org (e.g. President, Student Council)' : (state.template === 'academic' ? 'Strength / Activity' : 'Organization / Event')}" value="${esc(item.org)}" oninput="state.extracurricular[${i}].org=this.value; isPristine=false; render()">
                <input placeholder="${state.template === 'attorney' ? 'Role / Extra Details (Optional)' : 'Role (Optional)'}" value="${esc(item.role)}" oninput="state.extracurricular[${i}].role=this.value; isPristine=false; render()">
              </div>
              <div class="form-grid" style="margin-bottom:8px">
                <input placeholder="${state.template === 'attorney' ? 'Year (e.g. 2025)' : 'Date'}" value="${esc(item.date)}" oninput="state.extracurricular[${i}].date=this.value; isPristine=false; render()">
                <input placeholder="Link (URL, Optional)" value="${esc(item.link || '')}" oninput="state.extracurricular[${i}].link=this.value; isPristine=false; render()">
              </div>
              <div class="label-row" style="margin-top:8px;"><label style="font-size:10px; color:var(--text-muted);">Description</label><button class="btn-ai" onclick="rewriteText(event, 'extracurricular', ${i})">✨ Enhance</button></div>
              <textarea placeholder="Description (Supports multiline for bullets and **bold** text)" oninput="state.extracurricular[${i}].desc=this.value; isPristine=false; render()">${esc(item.desc)}</textarea>
            </div>`)
            .join("");
        }
        
        if(document.getElementById("skill-level-fields")) {
            document.getElementById("skill-level-fields").innerHTML = state.skillLevels.map((item, i) => `
                <div class="dynamic-item">
                    <button class="btn-del" onclick="remove('skillLevels', ${i})">×</button>
                    <div class="form-grid">
                        <input placeholder="Skill Name" value="${esc(item.name)}" oninput="state.skillLevels[${i}].name=this.value; render()">
                        <input type="number" min="0" max="100" placeholder="Level % (0-100)" value="${esc(item.level)}" oninput="state.skillLevels[${i}].level=this.value; render()">
                    </div>
                </div>
            `).join("");
        }
        if(document.getElementById("reference-fields")) {
            document.getElementById("reference-fields").innerHTML = state.references.map((item, i) => `
                <div class="dynamic-item">
                    <button class="btn-del" onclick="remove('references', ${i})">×</button>
                    <input placeholder="Reference Name" value="${esc(item.name)}" oninput="state.references[${i}].name=this.value; render()" style="margin-bottom:8px">
                    <div class="form-grid">
                        <input placeholder="Job Title" value="${esc(item.role)}" oninput="state.references[${i}].role=this.value; render()">
                        <input placeholder="Company Name" value="${esc(item.company)}" oninput="state.references[${i}].company=this.value; render()">
                    </div>
                </div>
            `).join("");
        }
      }

      // --- RENDER PREVIEW ---
      function render() {
        normalizeState();
        
        const p = document.getElementById("preview");
        const isAnimating = p.classList.contains("animating");
        p.className = `resume-page tmpl-${state.template} ${isAnimating ? "animating" : ""}`;

        const skillArr = state.skills ? state.skills.split(",").map((s) => s.trim()).filter(Boolean) : [];
        const langArr = state.languages ? state.languages.split(",").map((s) => s.trim()).filter(Boolean) : [];
        const hobArr = state.hobbies ? state.hobbies.split(",").map((s) => s.trim()).filter(Boolean) : [];
        const cwArr = state.coursework ? state.coursework.split(",").map((s) => s.trim()).filter(Boolean) : [];

        const education = state.education;
        const experience = state.experience;
        const projects = state.projects;
        const techSkills = state.techSkills;
        const achievements = state.achievements;
        const certifications = state.certifications;
        const extracurricular = state.extracurricular;

        if (state.template === "academic") {
          p.innerHTML = `
            <div class="header-area">
              <div class="header-left">
                ${state.name ? `<h1 class="name-header">${esc(state.name)}</h1>` : ""}
                ${state.role ? `<div class="role-title">${esc(state.role)}</div>` : ""}
              </div>
              ${(state.address || state.phone || state.email || state.linkedin) ? `
              <div class="contact-area">
                 ${[
                   state.address ? `<div style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:4px;">${icons.pin} ${esc(state.address)}</div>` : "",
                   state.linkedin ? `<div style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:4px;">${icons.linkedin} <a href="${getUrl(state.linkedin)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank">Linkedin</a></div>` : "",
                   state.email ? `<div style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:4px;">${icons.email} <a href="mailto:${esc(state.email)}" class="pdf-link">${esc(state.email)}</a></div>` : "",
                   state.phone ? `<div style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:4px;">${icons.phone} ${esc(state.phone)}</div>` : ""
                 ].filter(Boolean).join("")}
              </div>
              ` : ""}
            </div>

            <div class="grid-container">
              <div class="left-col">
                ${state.summary ? `
                <h2>PROFILE</h2>
                <p>${formatText(state.summary)}</p>
                ` : ""}

                ${experience.length > 0 ? `
                <h2>EXPERIENCE</h2>
                ${experience.map(e => `
                  <div class="item-wrap">
                    <div class="item-title">${esc(e.title)}</div>
                    <div class="item-subtitle">${esc(e.company)}</div>
                    <div class="item-date">
                      ${icons.calendar}
                      ${esc(e.date)}
                    </div>
                    <ul>${formatDescToLi(e.desc)}</ul>
                  </div>
                `).join('')}
                ` : ""}

                ${projects.length > 0 ? `
                <h2>PROJECTS</h2>
                ${projects.map(p => `
                  <div class="item-wrap">
                    <div class="item-title">${esc(p.title)}</div>
                    ${p.tech ? `<div class="item-subtitle">${esc(p.tech)}</div>` : ''}
                    ${p.date ? `
                    <div class="item-date">
                      ${icons.calendar}
                      ${esc(p.date || '')}
                    </div>
                    ` : ''}
                    ${p.link || p.liveLink ? `
                    <div style="font-size: 8.5pt; margin-bottom: 4pt;">
                      ${p.link ? `<a href="${getUrl(p.link)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:#555;text-decoration:none;"><u>GitHub</u></a>` : ''}
                      ${p.link && p.liveLink ? ' | ' : ''}
                      ${p.liveLink ? `<a href="${getUrl(p.liveLink)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:#555;text-decoration:none;"><u>Live</u></a>` : ''}
                    </div>` : ''}
                    <ul>${formatDescToLi(p.desc)}</ul>
                  </div>
                `).join('')}
                ` : ""}
              </div>

              <div class="right-col">
                ${skillArr.length > 0 ? `
                <h2>CORE SKILLS</h2>
                <div class="pill-container">
                  ${skillArr.map(s => `<div class="skill-pill">${esc(s)}</div>`).join('')}
                </div>
                ` : ""}

                ${techSkills.length > 0 ? `
                <h2>TECHNICAL SKILLS</h2>
                <div class="pill-container">
                  ${techSkills.map(ts => (ts.items || '').split(',').map(s => s.trim() ? `<div class="skill-pill">${esc(s.trim())}</div>` : '').join('')).join('')}
                </div>
                ` : ""}

                ${education.length > 0 ? `
                <h2>EDUCATION</h2>
                ${education.map(e => `
                  <div class="item-wrap" style="margin-bottom: 8pt;">
                    <div class="item-title" style="font-weight: 500;">${esc(e.degree)}</div>
                    <div class="item-subtitle" style="font-weight: 600;">${esc(e.school)}</div>
                    <div class="item-date" style="margin-top: 2pt;">
                      ${icons.calendar}
                      ${esc(e.date)}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                `).join('')}
                ` : ""}

                ${certifications.length > 0 ? `
                <h2>CERTIFICATIONS</h2>
                <ul class="clean-list">
                  ${certifications.map(c => `<li>${esc(c.name)} ${c.link ? `(<a href="${getUrl(c.link)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:#666; text-decoration:underline;">Link</a>)` : ''}</li>`).join('')}
                </ul>
                ` : ""}

                ${hobArr.length > 0 ? `
                <h2>HOBBIES</h2>
                <ul class="clean-list">
                  ${hobArr.map(h => `<li>${esc(h)}</li>`).join('')}
                </ul>
                ` : ""}

                ${extracurricular.length > 0 || achievements.length > 0 ? `
                <h2>ADDITIONAL STRENGTHS</h2>
                <ul class="clean-list">
                  ${extracurricular.map(e => `<li>${esc(e.org)} ${e.role ? `- ${esc(e.role)}` : ''}</li>`).join('')}
                  ${achievements.map(a => {
                    if(!a || typeof a !== 'string') return '';
                    return a.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim()).map(line => `<li>${formatText(line)}</li>`).join('');
                  }).join('')}
                </ul>
                ` : ""}
              </div>
            </div>
          `;
        } else if (state.template === "minimal") {
          p.innerHTML = `
            <div style="text-align: center; display: flex; flex-direction: column; align-items: center; gap: 4px; margin-bottom: 0;">
                <h1 class="resume-name" style="line-height: 0.75; margin: 0;">${esc(state.name)}</h1>
                ${state.address ? `<div style="font-size: 11.5pt; color: #000; line-height: 1; margin: 0;">${esc(state.address)}</div>` : ""}
                ${(state.phone || state.email || state.linkedin || state.github) ? `
                <div class="resume-contact-links" style="font-size: 10.5pt; display: flex; justify-content: center; align-items: center; gap: 14pt; flex-wrap: wrap; color: #000; margin: 0; line-height: 1;">
                  ${state.phone ? `<span style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:4px;">${icons.phone} <span class="contact-phone" style="position: relative; top: 1px;">${esc(state.phone)}</span></span>` : ""}
                  ${state.email ? `<span style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:4px;">${icons.email} <a href="mailto:${esc(state.email)}" class="pdf-link" style="color:#000; text-decoration:underline; text-underline-offset: 3px;">${esc(state.email)}</a></span>` : ""}
                  ${state.linkedin ? `<span style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:4px;">${icons.linkedin} <a href="${getUrl(state.linkedin)}" class="pdf-link" style="color:#000; text-decoration:underline; text-underline-offset: 3px;" target="_blank">LinkedIn</a></span>` : ""}
                  ${state.github ? `<span style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:4px;">${icons.github} <a href="${getUrl(state.github)}" class="pdf-link" style="color:#000; text-decoration:underline; text-underline-offset: 3px;" target="_blank">GitHub</a></span>` : ""}
                </div>
                ` : ""}
            </div>

            ${state.summary ? `
            <div class="section-title">Professional Summary</div>
            <p>${formatText(state.summary)}</p>
            ` : ""}

            ${education.length > 0 ? `
            <div class="section-title">Education</div>
            ${education.map(e => `
              <div style="margin-bottom: 3pt;">
                <div class="flex-between" style="margin-bottom: 1pt;">
                  <div style="flex: 1; min-width: 0; max-width: 78%; padding-right: 15px;"><strong>${esc(e.school)}</strong></div>
                  <div style="white-space: nowrap; flex-shrink: 0; text-align: right;"><strong>${esc(e.date)}</strong></div>
                </div>
                <div class="flex-between">
                  <div style="flex: 1; min-width: 0; max-width: 78%; padding-right: 15px;"><em>${esc(e.degree)}</em></div>
                  <div style="white-space: nowrap; flex-shrink: 0; text-align: right;"><em>${esc(e.location)}</em></div>
                </div>
              </div>
            `).join('')}
            ` : ""}

            ${cwArr.length > 0 ? `
            <div class="section-title">Relevant Coursework</div>
            <ul class="coursework-grid">
              ${cwArr.map(c => `<li>${esc(c)}</li>`).join('')}
            </ul>
            ` : ""}

            ${projects.length > 0 ? `
            <div class="section-title">Projects</div>
            ${projects.map(p => `
              <div style="margin-bottom: 4pt;">
                <div class="flex-between" style="margin-bottom: 1pt;">
                  <div style="flex: 1; min-width: 0; max-width: 78%; padding-right: 15px;">
                    <strong>${esc(p.title)}</strong>
                    ${p.tech ? `<span style="margin: 0 4px;">|</span><strong><em>${esc(p.tech)}</em></strong>` : ''}
                    ${p.link ? `<span style="margin: 0 4px;">|</span><a href="${getUrl(p.link)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:#000; text-decoration:underline; text-underline-offset: 3px;">GitHub</a>` : ''}
                    ${p.liveLink ? `<span style="margin: 0 4px;">|</span><a href="${getUrl(p.liveLink)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:#000; text-decoration:underline; text-underline-offset: 3px;">Live</a>` : ''}
                  </div>
                  <div style="white-space: nowrap; flex-shrink: 0; text-align: right;">${esc(p.date || '')}</div>
                </div>
                <ul style="margin-top: 2pt;">${formatDescToLi(p.desc)}</ul>
              </div>
            `).join('')}
            ` : ""}

            ${techSkills.length > 0 ? `
            <div class="section-title">Technical Skills</div>
            <div style="margin-bottom: 4pt;">
            ${techSkills.map(s => `
              <div style="margin-bottom: 1pt; margin-left: 16pt;">
                <strong>${esc(s.cat)}:</strong> ${esc(s.items)}
              </div>
            `).join('')}
            </div>
            ` : ""}

            ${certifications.length > 0 ? `
            <div class="section-title">Certifications</div>
            <ul>
            ${certifications.map(c => `
              <li style="margin-bottom: 2pt;">
                <div class="flex-between">
                  <div style="flex: 1; min-width: 0; max-width: 78%; padding-right: 15px;">${esc(c.name)} ${c.link ? `<a href="${getUrl(c.link)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:#000; text-decoration:underline; text-underline-offset: 3px;">(Certificate)</a>` : ''}</div>
                  <div style="white-space: nowrap; flex-shrink: 0; text-align: right;">${esc(c.date)}</div>
                </div>
              </li>
            `).join('')}
            </ul>
            ` : ""}

            ${extracurricular.length > 0 ? `
            <div class="section-title">Extracurricular</div>
            <ul>
            ${extracurricular.map(e => `
              <li style="margin-bottom: 2pt;">
                <div class="flex-between" style="margin-bottom: 2pt;">
                  <div style="flex: 1; min-width: 0; max-width: 78%; padding-right: 15px;"><strong>${e.link ? `<a href="${getUrl(e.link)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:inherit; text-decoration:none;">${esc(e.org)}</a>` : esc(e.org)}</strong>${e.role ? ` — <em>${esc(e.role)}</em>` : ''}</div>
                  <div style="white-space: nowrap; flex-shrink: 0; text-align: right;">${esc(e.date)}</div>
                </div>
                ${e.desc ? `<ul style="margin-top: 2pt;">${formatDescToLi(e.desc)}</ul>` : ''}
              </li>
            `).join('')}
            </ul>
            ` : ""}

            ${achievements.length > 0 ? `
            <div class="section-title">Achievements</div>
            <ul>
              ${achievements.map(a => {
                if(!a || typeof a !== 'string') return '';
                return formatDescToLi(a);
              }).join('')}
            </ul>
            ` : ""}
            
            ${experience.length > 0 ? `
            <div class="section-title">Experience</div>
            ${experience.map(e => `
              <div style="margin-bottom: 4pt;">
                <div class="flex-between" style="margin-bottom: 1pt;">
                  <div style="flex: 1; min-width: 0; max-width: 78%; padding-right: 15px;"><strong>${esc(e.title)}</strong></div>
                  <div style="white-space: nowrap; flex-shrink: 0; text-align: right;">${esc(e.date)}</div>
                </div>
                <div class="flex-between">
                  <div style="flex: 1; min-width: 0; max-width: 78%; padding-right: 15px;"><em>${esc(e.company)}</em></div>
                </div>
                <ul style="margin-top: 2pt;">${formatDescToLi(e.desc)}</ul>
              </div>
            `).join('')}
            ` : ""}
          `;
        } else if (state.template === "modern") {
          p.innerHTML = `
            <div class="sidebar" style="background: #292929; color: #e5e7eb; padding: 40pt 25pt;">
              ${state.photo ? `<img src="${state.photo}" class="pfp">` : ``}
              
              ${state.summary ? `
              <div class="sec-title-side">ABOUT ME</div>
              <div style="font-size: 9pt; line-height: 1.6; color: #ccc; margin-bottom: 30pt;">
                ${formatText(state.summary)}
              </div>` : ''}

              ${state.skillLevels && state.skillLevels.length > 0 ? `
              <div class="sec-title-side">SKILLS</div>
              <div class="side-timeline">
                ${state.skillLevels.map(s => `
                  <div class="side-item">
                    <div class="side-dot"></div>
                    <div style="font-size: 9pt; color: #fff; margin-bottom: 5pt; font-weight: 600;">${esc(s.name)}</div>
                    <div style="width: 100%; height: 4px; background: rgba(255,255,255,0.2);">
                      <div style="width: ${esc(s.level)}%; height: 100%; background: #fff;"></div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                `).join('')}
              </div>` : ''}

              ${state.references && state.references.length > 0 ? `
              <div class="sec-title-side">REFERENCE</div>
              <div class="side-timeline">
                ${state.references.map(r => `
                  <div class="side-item">
                    <div class="side-dot"></div>
                    <div style="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: 600; color: #fff; margin-bottom: 2pt;">${esc(r.name)}</div>
                    <div style="font-size: 8.5pt; color: #aaa; line-height: 1.4;">${esc(r.role)} | ${esc(r.company)}</div>
                  </div>
                `).join('')}
              </div>` : ''}

                        <div class="right-block body-text">${esc(e.date)}</div>

                        <div class="item-title" style="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: 700; color: #1e3a8a;">${esc(e.title)}</div>

                      </div>

                  <div class="section-title" style="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: 700; color: #71717a; text-transform: uppercase; border-bottom: 1px solid #e5e7eb; padding-bottom: 2pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; letter-spacing: 0.5px;">INTERESTS</div>
                  <div class="desc" style="margin-bottom: 12pt; font-size: 8.5pt; color: #4b5563; line-height: 1.35;">

              </div>
            </div>
          `;

              (state.photo ? "<div class=\"pod-photo-wrap\"><img src=\"" + state.photo + "\"></div>" : "") +

              "<div class=\"pod-left-col\">";

              "<div class=\"pod-sec-title\">" +
                  "<span>Profile</span>" +
              "</div>" +
              "<div class=\"pod-text-block\">" + formatText(state.summary) + "</div>";
          }

          if (experience.length > 0) {
              podHtml += "<div class=\"pod-sec-title\"><span>Experience</span></div>";
              experience.forEach(e => {
                  podHtml += "" +
                  "<div class=\"pod-item\">" +
                    "<div class=\"pod-item-top\">" +
                      "<div class=\"pod-item-title\">" + esc(e.title) + "</div>" +
                      "<div class=\"pod-item-date\">" + esc(e.date) + "</div>" +
                    "</div>" +
                    "<div class=\"pod-item-subtitle\">" + esc(e.company) + "</div>" +
                    "<ul class=\"pod-bullets\">" + formatDescToLi(e.desc) + "</ul>" +
                  "</div>";
              });
          }
          
          if (projects.length > 0) {
              podHtml += "<div class=\"pod-sec-title\"><span>Projects</span></div>";
              projects.forEach(pr => {
                  podHtml += "" +
                  "<div class=\"pod-item\">" +
                    "<div class=\"pod-item-top\">" +
                      "<div class=\"pod-item-title\">" + esc(pr.title) + "</div>" +
                      "<div class=\"pod-item-date\">" + esc(pr.date || '') + "</div>" +
                    "</div>" +
                    "<div class=\"pod-item-subtitle\" style=\"font-weight: 500;\">" +
                      (pr.tech ? esc(pr.tech) : '') +
                      (pr.link ? " | <a href=\"" + getUrl(pr.link) + "\" class=\"pdf-link\" target=\"_blank\">GitHub</a>" : '') +
                      (pr.liveLink ? " | <a href=\"" + getUrl(pr.liveLink) + "\" class=\"pdf-link\" target=\"_blank\">Live</a>" : '') +
                    "</div>" +
                    "<ul class=\"pod-bullets\">" + formatDescToLi(pr.desc) + "</ul>" +
                  "</div>";
              });
          }
          
          if (education.length > 0) {
              podHtml += "<div class=\"pod-sec-title\"><span>Education</span></div>";
              education.forEach(e => {
                  podHtml += "" +
                  "<div class=\"pod-item\">" +
                    "<div class=\"pod-item-top\">" +
                      "<div class=\"pod-item-title\">" + esc(e.degree) + "</div>" +
                      "<div class=\"pod-item-date\">" + esc(e.date) + "</div>" +
                    "</div>" +
                    "<div class=\"pod-item-subtitle\">" + esc(e.school) + "</div>" +
                    "<div class=\"pod-text-block\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0;\">" + esc(e.location) + "</div>" +
                  "</div>";
              });
          }

          podHtml += "</div><div class=\"pod-right\">";

          if (state.email || state.phone || state.linkedin || state.github || state.address) {
              podHtml += "<div class=\"pod-contact-block\">";
              if (state.address) podHtml += "<div class=\"pod-contact-row\"><span>" + esc(state.address) + "</span> " + icons.pin + "</div>";
              if (state.phone) podHtml += "<div class=\"pod-contact-row\"><span>" + esc(state.phone) + "</span> " + icons.phone + "</div>";
              if (state.email) podHtml += "<div class=\"pod-contact-row\"><a href=\"mailto:" + esc(state.email) + "\" class=\"pdf-link\">" + esc(state.email) + "</a> " + icons.email + "</div>";
              if (state.linkedin) podHtml += "<div class=\"pod-contact-row\"><a href=\"" + getUrl(state.linkedin) + "\" class=\"pdf-link\" target=\"_blank\">LinkedIn</a> " + icons.linkedin + "</div>";
              if (state.github) podHtml += "<div class=\"pod-contact-row\"><a href=\"" + getUrl(state.github) + "\" class=\"pdf-link\" target=\"_blank\">GitHub</a> " + icons.github + "</div>";
              podHtml += "</div>";
          }

          if (techSkills.length > 0 || skillArr.length > 0) {
              podHtml += "<div class=\"pod-sec-title\" style=\"margin-top: 0;\"><span>Skills</span></div><div class=\"pod-skills-wrap\">";
              if (skillArr.length > 0) {
                  skillArr.forEach(s => { podHtml += "<span class=\"pod-skill-pill\">" + esc(s) + "</span>"; });
              }
              techSkills.forEach(ts => {
                  let items = ts.items.split(',').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean);
                  items.forEach(s => { podHtml += "<span class=\"pod-skill-pill\">" + esc(s) + "</span>"; });
              });
              podHtml += "</div>";
          }

          if (certifications.length > 0) {
              podHtml += "<div class=\"pod-sec-title\"><span>Certifications</span></div>";
              certifications.forEach(c => {
                  let certName = formatText(esc(c.name));
                  if (c.link) certName = "<a href=\"" + getUrl(c.link) + "\" class=\"pdf-link\" target=\"_blank\">" + certName + "</a>";
                  podHtml += "" +
                  "<div class=\"pod-item\">" +
                    "<div class=\"pod-item-title\">" + certName + "</div>" +
                    "<div class=\"pod-item-date\" style=\"margin-top: 2px;\">" + esc(c.date) + "</div>" +
                  "</div>";
              });
          }
          
          if (achievements.length > 0) {
              podHtml += "<div class=\"pod-sec-title\"><span>Achievements</span></div><ul class=\"pod-bullets\" style=\"margin-bottom: 20pt;\">";
              achievements.forEach(a => {
                  if(a && typeof a === 'string') {
                      a.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim()).forEach(line => {
                          let cleaned = line.replace(/^[•\-]\s*/, '');
                          podHtml += "<li>" + formatText(cleaned) + "</li>";
                      });
                  }
              });
              podHtml += "</ul>";
          }

          if (extracurricular.length > 0) {
              podHtml += "<div class=\"pod-sec-title\"><span>Extracurricular</span></div>";
              extracurricular.forEach(e => {
                  podHtml += "" +
                  "<div class=\"pod-item\">" +
                    "<div class=\"pod-item-title\">" + esc(e.org) + "</div>" +
                    (e.role ? "<div class=\"pod-item-subtitle\" style=\"margin: 2px 0;\">" + esc(e.role) + "</div>" : "") +
                    "<div class=\"pod-item-date\" style=\"margin-bottom: 4px;\">" + esc(e.date) + "</div>" +
                    (e.desc ? "<div class=\"pod-text-block\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0;\">" + formatText(e.desc) + "</div>" : "") +
                  "</div>";
              });
          }

          podHtml += "</div></div>";
          p.innerHTML = podHtml;
        }
      }

      async function rewriteText(event, type, index = null) {
          const btn = event.currentTarget;
          let currentText = "";

          // Get current text based on field
          if (type === 'summary') currentText = state.summary;
          else if (type === 'experience') currentText = state.experience[index].desc;
          else if (type === 'projects') currentText = state.projects[index].desc;
          else if (type === 'extracurricular') currentText = state.extracurricular[index].desc;

          if (!currentText || currentText.trim() === "") {
              alert("Please write a draft first so the AI knows what to enhance!");
              return;
          }

          const originalHTML = btn.innerHTML;
          btn.innerHTML = "⏳ Enhancing...";
          btn.disabled = true;

          try {
              // Call your backend AI route
              const response = await fetch("http://localhost:5000/api/ai/rewrite", {
                  method: "POST",
                  headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
                  body: JSON.stringify({ 
                    text: currentText, 
                    context: type 
                  }),
              });

              if (!response.ok) throw new Error("Failed to connect to AI server.");

              const data = await response.json();
              
              // Assuming your backend sends the result back as { enhancedText: "..." }
              const enhancedText = data.enhancedText || data.text || data.result;

              if (enhancedText) {
                  isPristine = false;
                  if (type === 'summary') state.summary = enhancedText;
                  else if (type === 'experience') state.experience[index].desc = enhancedText;
                  else if (type === 'projects') state.projects[index].desc = enhancedText;
                  else if (type === 'extracurricular') state.extracurricular[index].desc = enhancedText;

                  renderInputs(); // Refresh the text boxes
                  render();       // Refresh the preview
              }
          } catch (err) {
              console.error("AI Enhance Error:", err);
              alert("Failed to enhance text. Make sure your server is running on port 5000.");
          } finally {
              btn.innerHTML = originalHTML;
              btn.disabled = false;
          }
      }

      async function saveResumeToDB() {
        const userId = localStorage.getItem("userId");
        const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
        const existingResumeId = urlParams.get("id");

        if (!state.name || !state.email) {
          alert("Name and Email are required to save!");
          return;
        }

        const payload = {
          userId: userId,
          resumeId: existingResumeId,
          personalInfo: {
            name: state.name,
            email: state.email,
            phone: state.phone,
          },
          templateType: state.template,
          templateSpecificInputs: state,
        };

        try {
          const response = await fetch("http://localhost:5000/api/resume", {
            method: "POST",
            headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
            body: JSON.stringify(payload),
          });

          const result = await response.json();

          if (response.ok) {
            alert("✅ Resume saved successfully!");
            if (!existingResumeId && result.data && result.data._id) {
              window.history.replaceState(
                null,
                "",
                `/editor.html?id=${result.data._id}`
              );
            }
          } else {
            alert("❌ Server Error: " + result.error);
          }
        } catch (error) {
          console.error("Save error:", error);
          alert("❌ Network Error: Is your server running on Port 5000?");
        }
      }

      async function loadResumeData(id) {
        try {
          const response = await fetch(`http://localhost:5000/api/resume/${id}`);
          if (!response.ok) throw new Error("Failed to load");

          const data = await response.json();

          if (data && data.templateSpecificInputs) {
            state = data.templateSpecificInputs;
            normalizeState();

            if (state.template) {
              document.getElementById("template-select").value = state.template;
              updateTemplate(state.template);
            }

            renderInputs();
            render();
          }
        } catch (error) {
          console.error("Error loading resume:", error);
          alert("Failed to load your saved resume data.");
        }
      }

      window.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
        const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
        const requestedTemplate = urlParams.get("template");
        const resumeId = urlParams.get("id");

        if (resumeId) {
          loadResumeData(resumeId);
        } else if (requestedTemplate) {
          document.getElementById("template-select").value = requestedTemplate;
          state.template = requestedTemplate;
          updateTemplate(requestedTemplate);
        } else {
          updateTemplate(document.getElementById("template-select").value);
        }

        renderInputs();
        render();
      });

      // 🚨 PERFECTED ALGORITHM: 1:1 LIVE DOM FLATTEN 🚨
      async function convertToStudio() {
          if (!localStorage.getItem("userId")) return alert("Please log in to use the Customizer Studio.");

          const preview = document.getElementById("preview");
          const btn = event.currentTarget || document.querySelector('[onclick="convertToStudio()"]');
          const originalText = btn.innerText;
          btn.innerText = "Exporting...";
          btn.disabled = true;

          // 1. Strip the animation BEFORE cloning to prevent scaling bugs
          preview.classList.remove("animating");
          preview.style.animation = "none";
          preview.style.transform = "none"; // Force 100% scale

          // Force browser to recalculate layout at true size
          void preview.offsetWidth;
          
          const parentRect = preview.getBoundingClientRect();
          let htmlStr = "";
          let zIndex = 10;
          let bgZIndex = 1;

          const getStyles = (el) => window.getComputedStyle(el);

          // Add base backgrounds based on template
          if (state.template === 'modern') {
              htmlStr += `<div class="element shape-element" style="left: 0px; top: 0px; width: 278px; height: 100%; background-color: #292929; z-index: 0;"></div>`;
          } else if (state.template === 'academic') {
              htmlStr += `<div class="element shape-element" style="left: 0px; top: 0px; width: 100%; height: 90px; background-color: transparent; z-index: 0;"></div>`;
          } else if (state.template === 'attorney') {
              htmlStr += `<div class="element shape-element" style="left: 0px; bottom: 0px; width: 100%; height: 90px; background-color: transparent; z-index: 0;"></div>`;
          } else if (state.template === 'innovative') {
              htmlStr += `<div class="element shape-element" style="left: 0px; top: 0px; width: 100%; height: 100%; background-color: #ffffff; z-index: 0;"></div>`;
          } else if (state.template === 'pod') {
              htmlStr += `<div class="element shape-element" style="left: 0px; top: 0px; width: 100%; height: 100%; background-color: #ffffff; z-index: 0;"></div>`;
          }

          // Measure the LIVE DOM node instead of a hidden wrapper clone to prevent flexbox squishing
          const walkDOM = (node) => {
              if (node.nodeType === 1) {
                  const tag = node.tagName.toLowerCase();
                  if (['script', 'style', 'svg', 'path', 'circle', 'rect', 'line', 'polygon'].includes(tag)) return;
                  
                  const styles = getStyles(node);
                  const r = node.getBoundingClientRect();

                  if (r.width === 0 || r.height === 0 || styles.display === 'none' || styles.visibility === 'hidden') return;

                  let l = r.left - parentRect.left;
                  let t = r.top - parentRect.top;

                  // 1. Extract Images
                  if (tag === 'img' || node.classList.contains('pfp') || node.parentElement.classList.contains('pod-photo-wrap')) {
                      htmlStr += `<div class="element image-element" style="left: ${l}px; top: ${t}px; width: ${r.width}px; height: ${r.height}px; border-radius: ${styles.borderRadius}; background-image: url('${node.src || state.photo}'); background-size: cover; z-index: ${zIndex++}; border: ${styles.borderWidth} solid ${styles.borderColor};"></div>`;
                      return; 
                  }

                  // 2. Extract UI Dots & Icons
                  if (node.classList.contains('timeline-dot') || node.classList.contains('side-dot') || node.classList.contains('dot') || node.classList.contains('ach-icon')) {
                      htmlStr += `<div class="element shape-element" style="left: ${l}px; top: ${t}px; width: ${r.width}px; height: ${r.height}px; border-radius: 50%; background-color: ${styles.backgroundColor}; border: ${styles.borderWidth} solid ${styles.borderColor}; z-index: ${zIndex++};"></div>`;
                      return; 
                  }

                  // 3. Extract Background Shapes (Sidebars, Topbars, Pills)
                  const bg = styles.backgroundColor;
                  if (bg !== 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)' && bg !== 'transparent' && !node.classList.contains('resume-page')) {
                      htmlStr += `<div class="element shape-element" style="left: ${l}px; top: ${t}px; width: ${r.width}px; height: ${r.height}px; border-radius: ${styles.borderRadius}; background-color: ${bg}; border: ${styles.borderWidth} solid ${styles.borderColor}; z-index: ${bgZIndex++};"></div>`;
                  }

                  // 4. Extract Lines (Borders)
                  if (parseFloat(styles.borderBottomWidth) > 0 && styles.borderBottomStyle !== 'none') {
                      htmlStr += `<div class="element shape-element" style="left: ${l}px; top: ${t + r.height - parseFloat(styles.borderBottomWidth)}px; width: ${r.width}px; height: ${parseFloat(styles.borderBottomWidth)}px; background-color: ${styles.borderBottomColor}; z-index: 5;"></div>`;
                  }
                  if (parseFloat(styles.borderLeftWidth) > 0 && styles.borderLeftStyle !== 'none' && !node.classList.contains('side-timeline') && !node.classList.contains('timeline')) {
                      htmlStr += `<div class="element shape-element" style="left: ${l}px; top: ${t}px; width: ${parseFloat(styles.borderLeftWidth)}px; height: ${r.height}px; background-color: ${styles.borderLeftColor}; z-index: 5;"></div>`;
                  }

                  // 5. Extract Text Blocks Safely
                  let containsBlock = false;
                  let hasText = false;
                  
                  for (let child of node.childNodes) {
                      if (child.nodeType === 3 && child.nodeValue.trim().length > 0) hasText = true;
                      if (child.nodeType === 1) {
                          const d = getStyles(child).display;
                          if (d === 'block' || d === 'flex' || d === 'grid' || d === 'table' || d === 'list-item') {
                              containsBlock = true;
                              break;
                          }
                      }
                  }

                  if (!containsBlock && (hasText || node.innerText.trim() !== '')) {
                      let content = node.innerHTML;
                      if (tag === 'li') {
                          if (state.template === 'attorney') content = "– " + content;
                          else if (state.template === 'pod') content = "• " + content; // Bullet logic applied here too
                          else content = "• " + content;
                      } 
                      
                      // Explicitly capture all typography so it survives the transfer exactly as designed
                      const fontFam = styles.fontFamily.replace(/"/g, "'");
                      const ls = styles.letterSpacing === 'normal' ? '0px' : styles.letterSpacing;
                      const tt = styles.textTransform;
                      const fs = styles.fontStyle;
                      const fw = styles.fontWeight;
                      const fSize = styles.fontSize;
                      const lh = styles.lineHeight;
                      const ta = styles.textAlign;
                      const color = styles.color;
                      
                      // We give the width an extra 15px buffer to stop text from wrapping prematurely 
                      htmlStr += `<div class="element text-element" contenteditable="false" spellcheck="false" style="left: ${l}px; top: ${t}px; width: ${r.width + 15}px; font-size: ${fSize}; font-weight: ${fw}; font-style: ${fs}; color: ${color}; font-family: ${fontFam}; text-align: ${ta}; line-height: ${lh}; letter-spacing: ${ls}; text-transform: ${tt}; white-space: pre-wrap; z-index: ${zIndex++};">${content}</div>`;
                      return; // Stop recursion for this branch
                  }

                  // Recurse children
                  for (let child of node.childNodes) {
                      walkDOM(child);
                  }
              }
          };

          walkDOM(preview);

          // Restore the preview scaling back to fit the window
          preview.style.transform = "";
          preview.style.transition = "";

          // Export to Customize via LocalStorage
          try {
              localStorage.setItem("tempStudioHtml", htmlStr);
              localStorage.setItem("tempStudioHeight", "1123"); 
              window.location.href = "customize.html?mode=temp";
          } catch (e) {
              console.error(e);
              alert("Network error while exporting.");
              btn.innerText = originalText;
              btn.disabled = false;
          }
      }
    </script>
  </body>
</html>

    <script>

    /* ── Toast system ── */
    function showToast(type, title, msg, duration) {
      const container = document.getElementById('toast-container');
      const icons = { success: '✓', error: '✕', info: 'i', warning: '!' };
      const toast = document.createElement('div');
      toast.className = 'toast ' + type;
      toast.innerHTML = `
        <div class="toast-icon">${icons[type] || 'i'}</div>
        <div class="toast-body">
          <div class="toast-title">${title}</div>
          ${msg ? `<div class="toast-msg">${msg}</div>` : ''}
        </div>
        <button class="toast-close" onclick="dismissToast(this.parentElement)">✕</button>
      `;
      container.appendChild(toast);
      const t = duration || (type === 'error' ? 5000 : 3500);
      setTimeout(() => dismissToast(toast), t);
    }
    function dismissToast(el) {
      if (!el || el.classList.contains('toast-out')) return;
      el.classList.add('toast-out');
      setTimeout(() => el.remove(), 220);
    }

    /* ── Confirm modal ── */
    let _confirmResolve = null;
    function showConfirm(title, msg, okLabel) {
      document.getElementById('confirm-title').textContent = title || 'Are you sure?';
      document.getElementById('confirm-message').textContent = msg || '';
      if (okLabel) document.querySelector('#confirm-actions .ok').textContent = okLabel;
      document.getElementById('confirm-overlay').classList.add('visible');
      return new Promise(res => { _confirmResolve = res; });
    }
    function resolveConfirm(val) {
      document.getElementById('confirm-overlay').classList.remove('visible');
      if (_confirmResolve) { _confirmResolve(val); _confirmResolve = null; }
    }
    document.getElementById('confirm-overlay').addEventListener('click', function(e) {
      if (e.target === this) resolveConfirm(false);
    });

    /* ── Link display toggle (label vs url) ── */
    function toggleLinkDisplay(type) {
      const cur = state[type + 'Display'] || 'label';
      state[type + 'Display'] = cur === 'label' ? 'url' : 'label';
      state._touched[type + 'Display'] = true;
      const btn = document.getElementById(type + '-display-btn');
      if (btn) btn.textContent = state[type + 'Display'] === 'url' ? 'URL' : 'Label';
      render();
    }

    /* ── Custom select ── */
    function toggleCustomSelect() {
      const wrap = document.getElementById('template-select-wrap');
      const isOpen = wrap.classList.contains('open');
      wrap.classList.toggle('open', !isOpen);
    }
    function pickTemplate(val, el) {
      const menu = document.getElementById('template-select-menu');
      const trigger = document.getElementById('template-select-trigger');
      menu.querySelectorAll('.custom-select-option').forEach(o => o.classList.remove('selected'));
      el.classList.add('selected');
      trigger.textContent = el.textContent.trim();
      document.getElementById('template-select-wrap').classList.remove('open');
      updateTemplate(val);
    }
    document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
      const wrap = document.getElementById('template-select-wrap');
      if (wrap && !wrap.contains(e.target)) wrap.classList.remove('open');
    });


    function initAll() {
        const storedName = localStorage.getItem('userName');
        const greetingElement = document.getElementById("user-greeting");
        if (storedName && greetingElement) {
            const cleanName = storedName.trim().split(' ')[0];
            const capitalized = cleanName.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + cleanName.slice(1);
            greetingElement.innerText = `Welcome, ${capitalized}`;
        } else if (greetingElement) {
            greetingElement.innerText = `Welcome!`;
        }

        // ── CHANGE 3: Horizontal resize handle logic ──
        const handle = document.getElementById("resize-handle");
        const editor = document.getElementById("editor");
        let isResizing = false;
        let startX = 0;
        let startWidth = 0;

        handle.addEventListener("mousedown", (e) => {
            isResizing = true;
            startX = e.clientX;
            startWidth = editor.offsetWidth;
            handle.classList.add("dragging");
            document.body.style.userSelect = "none";
            document.body.style.pointerEvents = "none";
            handle.style.pointerEvents = "auto";
        });

        document.addEventListener("mousemove", (e) => {
            if (!isResizing) return;
            const dx = e.clientX - startX;
            const newWidth = Math.min(700, Math.max(320, startWidth + dx));
            editor.style.width = newWidth + "px";
            document.documentElement.style.setProperty("--editor-width", newWidth + "px");
        });

        document.addEventListener("mouseup", () => {
            if (!isResizing) return;
            isResizing = false;
            handle.classList.remove("dragging");
            document.body.style.userSelect = "";
            document.body.style.pointerEvents = "";
            handle.style.pointerEvents = "";
        });
    }

    async function analyzeResume() {
      const job = document.getElementById("dream-job").value;
      const btn = document.getElementById("ai-analyze-btn");
      const resultArea = document.getElementById("ai-result-area");
      
      const scoreNumber = document.getElementById("ai-score-number");
          const atsNumber = document.getElementById("ai-ats-number");
      
      const suggestionsDiv = document.getElementById("ai-suggestions");

      if (!job) return showToast("warning","Missing Field","Please enter your dream job first.");

      btn.innerText = "Analyzing...";
      btn.disabled = true;

      try {
          const resumeText = document.getElementById("preview").innerText;

          const response = await fetch("/api/ai/analyze", {
              method: "POST",
              headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
              body: JSON.stringify({ jobTitle: job, resumeData: resumeText }),
          });

          if (!response.ok) throw new Error("Server responded with an error");

          const data = await response.json();
          console.log("📥 AI Data:", data);

          if (resultArea) resultArea.style.display = "block";

        

        function animateBar(numEl, barEl, target) {
            if (!numEl || !barEl) return;
            const hue = (target / 100) * 120;
            const color = `hsl(${hue}, 88%, 55%)`;
            numEl.innerText = '0';
            barEl.style.transition = 'none';
            barEl.style.width = '0%';
            void barEl.offsetWidth;
            setTimeout(() => {
              barEl.style.transition = 'width 1.5s cubic-bezier(0.4,0,0.2,1)';
              barEl.style.width = target + '%';
              numEl.style.color = color;
              let cur = 0, step = target / 90;
              const t = setInterval(() => {
                cur = Math.min(cur + step, target);
                numEl.innerText = Math.round(cur);
                if (cur >= target) clearInterval(t);
              }, 16);
            }, 60);
          }

          const rawScore = parseInt(data.score || data.jobScore || 0);
          animateBar(scoreNumber, document.getElementById('ai-score-bar'), rawScore);

          const rawAts = parseInt(data.atsScore || data.ats_score || data.ATS || 0);
          animateBar(atsNumber, document.getElementById('ai-ats-bar'), rawAts);

         if (suggestionsDiv) {
            if (data.suggestions) {
              const raw = data.suggestions
                .replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '$1')  // strip bold markers
                .replace(/\*/g, '')                 // strip stray asterisks
                .replace(/#+\s*/g, '')              // strip markdown headers
                .trim();

              // Split into points: by newline OR by sentence endings followed by capital
              const points = raw
                .split(/\n+/)
                .flatMap(line => line.split(/(?<=[.!?])\s+(?=[A-Z])/))
                .map(p => p.replace(/^[-•▸*\d.]+\s*/, '').trim())
                .filter(p => p.length > 8);

              let html = '';
              points.forEach(point => {
                // Detect if it looks like a section label (short, no period)
                if (point.length < 40 && !point.includes('.') && point === point.toUpperCase()) {
                  html += `<div style="margin: 20px 0 8px 0; padding-bottom: 6px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(196,85,118,0.25);">
                    <span style="font-size: 0.7rem; font-weight: 800; color: var(--rose-light); letter-spacing: 1.5px;">${point}</span>
                  </div>`;
                } else {
                  html += `<div style="display:flex; gap:12px; align-items:flex-start; margin-bottom:8px; padding:11px 14px; background:rgba(255,255,255,0.03); border-radius:8px; border-left:2px solid rgba(196,85,118,0.3);">
                    <span style="color:var(--rose-light); flex-shrink:0; margin-top:3px; font-size:0.7rem;">▸</span>
                    <span style="font-size:0.875rem; color:rgba(240,234,240,0.88); line-height:1.65;">${point}</span>
                  </div>`;
                }
              });

              suggestionsDiv.innerHTML = html || `<p style="color:rgba(240,234,240,0.5); font-style:italic;">No suggestions found.</p>`;
            } else {
              suggestionsDiv.innerHTML = `<p style="color:rgba(240,234,240,0.5); font-style:italic;">No specific suggestions found.</p>`;
            }
          }

          if (resultArea) {
  // On mobile, open the preview panel first, then scroll
  const previewWrap = document.getElementById('preview-wrap');
  const btn = document.getElementById('mobile-preview-btn');
  if (previewWrap && !previewWrap.classList.contains('mobile-visible') && window.innerWidth <= 1024) {
    previewWrap.classList.add('mobile-visible');
    if (btn) btn.innerHTML = `<svg width="13" height="13" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><line x1="18" y1="6" x2="6" y2="18"/><line x1="6" y1="6" x2="18" y2="18"/></svg> Close`;
    // Wait for the slide-in transition (350ms) before scrolling
    setTimeout(() => resultArea.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth" }), 380);
  } else {
    resultArea.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth" });
  }
}
      } catch (err) {
          console.error("Audit Error:", err);
          showToast("error","Connection Failed","Could not reach the AI server.");
      } finally {
          if (btn) {
              btn.innerText = "Audit";
              btn.disabled = false;
          }
      }
    }

    function toggleTheme() {
        const body = document.body;
        const icon = document.getElementById("theme-icon");
        if (body.getAttribute("data-theme") === "dark") {
            body.removeAttribute("data-theme");
            icon.innerHTML = '<path d="M21 12.79A9 9 0 1 1 11.21 3 7 7 0 0 0 21 12.79z"></path>';
        } else {
            body.setAttribute("data-theme", "dark");
            icon.innerHTML = '<circle cx="12" cy="12" r="5"></circle><line x1="12" y1="1" x2="12" y2="3"></line><line x1="12" y1="21" x2="12" y2="23"></line><line x1="4.22" y1="4.22" x2="5.64" y2="5.64"></line><line x1="18.36" y1="18.36" x2="19.78" y2="19.78"></line><line x1="1" y1="12" x2="3" y2="12"></line><line x1="21" y1="12" x2="23" y2="12"></line><line x1="4.22" y1="19.78" x2="5.64" y2="18.36"></line><line x1="18.36" y1="5.64" x2="19.78" y2="4.22"></line>';
        }
    }

   function downloadResumePDF() {
      const overlay = document.getElementById("print-overlay");
      const preview = document.getElementById("preview");

      if (overlay) overlay.classList.add("visible");
      preview.classList.remove("animating");

      requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        requestAnimationFrame(() => {
          if (overlay) overlay.classList.remove("visible");
          setTimeout(() => {
            window.print();
          }, 80);
        });
      });
    }

    function signOut() {
        localStorage.removeItem("userId");
        localStorage.removeItem("token");
        localStorage.removeItem("userName");
    }

    window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
        initAll();
    });

   function freshTemplateState() {
      return {
        photo: "", name: "", role: "", email: "", phone: "", address: "",
        linkedin: "", github: "", summary: "", refs: "", tagline: "",
        linkedinDisplay: "label", githubDisplay: "label",
        education: [], experience: [], projects: [], techSkills: [],
        achievements: [], skills: "", languages: "", hobbies: "",
        coursework: "", certifications: [], extracurricular: [],
        skillLevels: [], references: [],
        _touched: {} 
      };
    }

    let templateStates = {};
    TEMPLATES.forEach(t => { templateStates[t] = freshTemplateState(); });

    let currentTemplate = "academic";

    const state = new Proxy({}, {
      get(_, key) {
        if (key === "template") return currentTemplate;
        if (key === "_touched") return templateStates[currentTemplate]._touched;
        return templateStates[currentTemplate][key];
      },
      set(_, key, val) {
        if (key === "template") { currentTemplate = val; return true; }
        templateStates[currentTemplate][key] = val;
        templateStates[currentTemplate]._touched[key] = true; 
        return true;
      }
    });

      const iconStyle = `width: 10px; height: 10px; fill: currentColor; display: inline-block; vertical-align: middle; margin-right: 4px; position: relative; top: -1px;`;
      const icons = {
        pin: `<svg style="${iconStyle}" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M12 0c-4.198 0-8 3.403-8 7.602 0 4.198 3.469 9.21 8 16.398 4.531-7.188 8-12.2 8-16.398 0-4.199-3.801-7.602-8-7.602zm0 11c-1.657 0-3-1.343-3-3s1.343-3 3-3 3 1.343 3-3 3-1.343 3-3 3z"/></svg>`,
       phone: `<svg style="${iconStyle}" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor"><path d="M6.6 10.8c1.4 2.8 3.8 5.1 6.6 6.6l2.2-2.2c.3-.3.7-.4 1-.2 1.1.4 2.3.6 3.6.6.6 0 1 .4 1 1V20c0 .6-.4 1-1 1C10.6 21 3 13.4 3 4c0-.6.4-1 1-1h3.5c.6 0 1 .4 1 1 0 1.3.2 2.5.6 3.6.1.3 0 .7-.2 1L6.6 10.8z"/></svg>`,
        email: `<svg style="${iconStyle}" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M20 4H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v12c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h16c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V6c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm0 4l-8 5-8-5V6l8 5 8-5v2z"/></svg>`,
        linkedin: `<svg style="${iconStyle}" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor"><path d="M19 0h-14c-2.761 0-5 2.239-5 5v14c0 2.761 2.239 5 5 5h14c2.762 0 5-2.239 5-5v-14c0-2.761-2.238-5-5-5zm-11 19h-3v-11h3v11zm-1.5-12.268c-.966 0-1.75-.79-1.75-1.764s.784-1.764 1.75-1.764 1.75.79 1.75 1.764-.783 1.764-1.75 1.764zm13.5 12.268h-3v-5.604c0-3.368-4-3.113-4 0v5.604h-3v-11h3v1.765c1.396-2.586 7-2.777 7 2.476v6.759z"/></svg>`,
        github: `<svg style="${iconStyle}" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor"><path d="M12 0c-6.626 0-12 5.373-12 12 0 5.302 3.438 9.8 8.207 11.387.599.111.793-.261.793-.577v-2.234c-3.338.726-4.033-1.416-4.033-1.416-.546-1.387-1.333-1.756-1.333-1.756-1.089-.745.083-.729.083-.729 1.205.084 1.839 1.237 1.839 1.237 1.07 1.834 2.807 1.304 3.492.997.107-.775.418-1.305.762-1.604-2.665-.305-5.467-1.334-5.467-5.931 0-1.311.469-2.381 1.236-3.221-.124-.303-.535-1.524.117-3.176 0 0 1.008-.322 3.301 1.23.957-.266 1.983-.399 3.003-.404 1.02.005 2.047.138 3.006.404 2.291-1.552 3.297-1.23 3.297-1.23.653 1.653.242 2.874.118 3.176.77.84 1.235 1.911 1.235 3.221 0 4.609-2.807 5.624-5.479 5.921.43.372.823 1.102.823 2.222v3.293c0 .319.192.694.801.576 4.765-1.589 8.199-6.086 8.199-11.386 0-6.627-5.373-12-12-12z"/></svg>`,
        calendar: `<svg style="${iconStyle}" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><rect x="3" y="4" width="18" height="18" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><line x1="16" y1="2" x2="16" y2="6"></line><line x1="8" y1="2" x2="8" y2="6"></line><line x1="3" y1="10" x2="21" y2="10"></line></svg>`
      };

      function getUrl(url) {
        let u = esc(url).trim();
        if(u && !u.startsWith('http') && !u.startsWith('mailto:')) return 'https://' + u;
        return u;
      }

      function isTextLink(item) {
        return item && item.linkType === 'textlink';
      }

      function buildSeparateLink(item, isAttorney, defaultLabel) {
        if (!item.link) return '';
        const label = esc(item.linkText || defaultLabel || 'Link');
        const url = getUrl(item.link);
        if (isAttorney) {
          return ` <a href="${url}" class="pdf-link inline-link" target="_blank">${label}</a>`;
        }
        return ` (<a href="${url}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:inherit; text-decoration:underline; text-underline-offset:3px;">${label}</a>)`;
      }

      function wrapWithLink(html, item, extraStyle) {
        if (!item.link || !isTextLink(item)) return html;
        const url = getUrl(item.link);
        const style = extraStyle || 'color:inherit; text-decoration:none;';
        return `<a href="${url}" class="pdf-link-inline" target="_blank" style="${style}">${html}</a>`;
      }

      function getAchievementText(a) {
        if (typeof a === 'string') return a;
        const textPart = a.text || '';
        const descPart = a.desc ? ' \u2013 ' + a.desc : '';
        return textPart + descPart;
      }

     function normalizeState() {
        const ts = templateStates[currentTemplate];
        
        if (!ts._touched) {
            ts._touched = {};
        }
        
        // We write directly to 'ts' instead of 'state' to bypass the Proxy. 
        // This stops it from accidentally marking fields as "touched" by the user!
        ts.education = ts.education || [];
        ts.experience = ts.experience || [];
        ts.projects = ts.projects || [];
        ts.techSkills = ts.techSkills || [];
        ts.achievements = ts.achievements || [];
        ts.certifications = ts.certifications || [];
        ts.extracurricular = ts.extracurricular || [];
        ts.coursework = ts.coursework || "";
        ts.skills = ts.skills || "";
        ts.languages = ts.languages || "";
        ts.hobbies = ts.hobbies || "";
        ts.summary = ts.summary || "";
       ts.refs = ts.refs || "";
        ts.tagline = ts.tagline || "";
        ts.skillLevels = ts.skillLevels || [];
        ts.references = ts.references || [];
      }

      function esc(str) {
        if (!str) return "";
        return String(str)
          .replace(/&/g, "&amp;")
          .replace(/</g, "&lt;")
          .replace(/>/g, "&gt;")
          .replace(/"/g, "&quot;");
      }

      function formatText(text) {
