        if (!text) return "";
        return esc(text).replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, "<strong>$1</strong>");
      }

     function formatDescToLi(desc) {
        if (!desc) return "";
        return desc.split('\n')
          .map(line => line.trim())
          .filter(line => line.length > 0)
          .map(line => {
              let cleanedLine = line.replace(/^(?:[•–—\-]|\*(?!\*))\s*/, '');
              return `<li>${formatText(cleanedLine)}</li>`;
          })
          .join('');
      }

      function triggerPreviewAnimation() {
        const p = document.getElementById("preview");
        p.classList.remove("animating");
        void p.offsetWidth;
        p.classList.add("animating");
      }

     function updateTemplate(val) {
  currentTemplate = val;
 
  document.querySelectorAll("[data-show]").forEach((el) => {
    const allowed = el.getAttribute("data-show").split(",");
    el.style.display = allowed.includes(currentTemplate)
      ? (el.getAttribute("data-display") || "block")
      : "none";
  });
 
  // Re-render inputs from THIS template's state (could be empty = clean slate)
  renderInputs();
  render();
  triggerPreviewAnimation();
}

      function update(key, val) {
        state[key] = val;
        render();
      }

      function add(type) {
        normalizeState();
        state._touched[type] = true; 
        if (type === "experience")
          state.experience.push({ title: "", company: "", date: "", desc: "", link: "", linkText: "", linkType: "separate" });
        if (type === "education")
          state.education.push({ school: "", degree: "", date: "", location: "" });
        if (type === "projects")
          state.projects.push({ title: "", tech: "", link: "", liveLink: "", desc: "" });
        if (type === "techSkills")
          state.techSkills.push({ cat: "", items: "" });
        if (type === "achievements")
          state.achievements.push({ text: '', date: '', desc: '', link: '', linkText: '', linkType: 'separate' });
        if (type === "certifications") 
          state.certifications.push({ name: "", date: "", link: "", linkText: "", linkType: "separate" });
        if (type === "extracurricular")
          state.extracurricular.push({ org: "", role: "", date: "", desc: "", link: "", linkText: "", linkType: "separate" });
        if (type === "skillLevels")
          state.skillLevels.push({ name: "", level: "50" });
        if (type === "references")
          state.references.push({ name: "", role: "", company: "" });
        
        renderInputs();
        render();
      }

      function remove(type, i) {
        state[type].splice(i, 1);
        state._touched[type] = true; 
        renderInputs();
        render();
      }

      async function clearAll() {
        const ok = await showConfirm(
          "Clear current template?",
          "This will remove all content for the current template. Other templates are not affected.",
          "Yes, clear"
        );
        if (ok) {
          templateStates[currentTemplate] = freshTemplateState();
          Object.keys(SAMPLE_DATA).forEach(k => {
             templateStates[currentTemplate]._touched[k] = true;
          });
          renderInputs();
          render();
          showToast("success", "Cleared", "Current template data has been cleared.");
        }
      }

   function handleImg(input) {
  if (!input.files || !input.files[0]) return;
  const reader = new FileReader();
  reader.onload = (e) => {
    state.photo = e.target.result;
    updateImageUI();
    render();
  };
  reader.readAsDataURL(input.files[0]);
  input.value = ""; // Reset input so the same file can be re-selected if removed
}

function removeImg() {
  state.photo = "";
  updateImageUI();
  render();
}

function updateImageUI() {
  const zone = document.getElementById('img-upload-zone');
  const preview = document.getElementById('img-preview-zone');
  const thumb = document.getElementById('img-preview-thumb');
  
  if (zone && preview && thumb) {
    if (state.photo) {
      zone.style.display = 'none';
      preview.style.display = 'flex';
      thumb.src = state.photo;
    } else {
      zone.style.display = 'flex';
      preview.style.display = 'none';
      thumb.src = '';
    }
  }
}

      function buildLinkTypeToggle(type, i, currentVal) {
        const val = currentVal || 'separate';
        const uid = `lt_${type}_${i}`;
        return `
          <div style="margin-bottom: 6px;">
            <label style="margin-bottom: 4px;">Link Style</label>
            <div class="link-type-toggle">
              <input type="radio" name="${uid}" id="${uid}_sep" value="separate" ${val === 'separate' ? 'checked' : ''} onchange="state.${type}[${i}].linkType='separate'; render();">
              <label for="${uid}_sep">Separate Link</label>
              <input type="radio" name="${uid}" id="${uid}_txt" value="textlink" ${val === 'textlink' ? 'checked' : ''} onchange="state.${type}[${i}].linkType='textlink'; render();">
              <label for="${uid}_txt">Title as Link</label>
            </div>
          </div>`;
      }

      function buildLinkFields(type, i, item, urlPlaceholder, labelPlaceholder) {
        const lt = item.linkType || 'separate';
        if (lt === 'textlink') {
          return `
            <div class="full-width" style="grid-column: span 2; margin-top: 4px;">
              <label>Link URL</label>
              <input placeholder="${urlPlaceholder || 'https://...'}" value="${esc(item.link || '')}" oninput="state.${type}[${i}].link=this.value; render();">
            </div>`;
        }
        return `
          <div style="margin-top: 4px;">
            <label>Link URL</label>
            <input placeholder="${urlPlaceholder || 'https://...'}" value="${esc(item.link || '')}" oninput="state.${type}[${i}].link=this.value; render();">
          </div>
          <div style="margin-top: 4px;">
            <label>Link Label</label>
            <input placeholder="${labelPlaceholder || 'e.g. Certificate, View'}" value="${esc(item.linkText || '')}" oninput="state.${type}[${i}].linkText=this.value; render();">
          </div>`;
      }

      function renderInputs() {
  normalizeState();
 
  document.getElementById("in-name").value = state.name;
  if (document.getElementById("in-tagline")) document.getElementById("in-tagline").value = state.tagline || '';
  document.getElementById("in-role").value = state.role;
  document.getElementById("in-phone").value = state.phone;
  document.getElementById("in-email").value = state.email;
  document.getElementById("in-linkedin").value = state.linkedin;
  document.getElementById("in-github").value = state.github;
  document.getElementById("in-address").value = state.address;
  document.getElementById("in-summary").value = state.summary;
  if (document.getElementById("in-refs")) document.getElementById("in-refs").value = state.refs;
  document.getElementById("in-skills").value = state.skills;
  if (document.getElementById("in-languages")) document.getElementById("in-languages").value = state.languages;
  document.getElementById("in-hobbies").value = state.hobbies;
  if (document.getElementById("in-coursework")) document.getElementById("in-coursework").value = state.coursework || '';
 
  document.getElementById("edu-fields").innerHTML = state.education
    .map((item, i) => `
    <div class="dynamic-item">
      <button class="btn-del" onclick="remove('education', ${i})" title="Remove">✕</button>
      <input placeholder="School / College" value="${esc(item.school)}" oninput="state.education[${i}].school=this.value; render()" style="margin-bottom:8px">
      <input placeholder="Degree / Details" value="${esc(item.degree)}" oninput="state.education[${i}].degree=this.value; render()" style="margin-bottom:8px">
      <div class="form-grid">
        <input placeholder="Dates" value="${esc(item.date)}" oninput="state.education[${i}].date=this.value; render()">
        ${currentTemplate !== 'academic' ? `<input placeholder="Location" value="${esc(item.location)}" oninput="state.education[${i}].location=this.value; render()">` : ''}
        ${currentTemplate === 'bordered' ? `<input placeholder="GPA / Percentage / Rank" value="${esc(item.gpa||'')}" oninput="state.education[${i}].gpa=this.value; render()">` : ''}
      </div>
    </div>`)
    .join("");
 
  document.getElementById("exp-fields").innerHTML = state.experience
    .map((item, i) => `
    <div class="dynamic-item">
      <button class="btn-del" onclick="remove('experience', ${i})" title="Remove">✕</button>
      <input placeholder="Job Title" value="${esc(item.title)}" oninput="state.experience[${i}].title=this.value; render()" style="margin-bottom:8px">
      <div class="form-grid" style="margin-bottom:8px"><input placeholder="Company" value="${esc(item.company)}" oninput="state.experience[${i}].company=this.value; render()"><input placeholder="Dates" value="${esc(item.date)}" oninput="state.experience[${i}].date=this.value; render()"></div>
      <div class="label-row" style="margin-top:8px;"><label style="font-size:12px; color:#a094a0;">Description</label><button class="btn-ai" onclick="rewriteText(event, 'experience', ${i})">✨ Enhance</button></div>
      <textarea placeholder="Description (Supports multiline for bullets and **bold** text)" oninput="state.experience[${i}].desc=this.value; render()">${esc(item.desc)}</textarea>
      <div class="form-grid" style="margin-top: 10px;">
        ${buildLinkTypeToggle('experience', i, item.linkType)}
      </div>
      <div class="form-grid">
        ${buildLinkFields('experience', i, item, 'https://...', 'e.g. Project, Demo')}
      </div>
    </div>`)
    .join("");
 
  document.getElementById("proj-fields").innerHTML = state.projects
    .map((item, i) => `
    <div class="dynamic-item">
      <button class="btn-del" onclick="remove('projects', ${i})" title="Remove">✕</button>
      <div class="form-grid" style="margin-bottom:8px">
        <input placeholder="Project Name" value="${esc(item.title)}" oninput="state.projects[${i}].title=this.value; render()">
        <input placeholder="Date (e.g. Oct 2023)" value="${esc(item.date || '')}" oninput="state.projects[${i}].date=this.value; render()">
      </div>
      <input placeholder="Tech Used" value="${esc(item.tech)}" oninput="state.projects[${i}].tech=this.value; render()" style="margin-bottom:8px">
      <div class="form-grid" style="margin-bottom:8px"><input placeholder="GitHub Link" value="${esc(item.link)}" oninput="state.projects[${i}].link=this.value; render()"><input placeholder="Live Link (Optional)" value="${esc(item.liveLink || '')}" oninput="state.projects[${i}].liveLink=this.value; render()"></div>
      <div class="label-row" style="margin-top:8px;"><label style="font-size:12px; color:#a094a0;">Description</label><button class="btn-ai" onclick="rewriteText(event, 'projects', ${i})">✨ Enhance</button></div>
      <textarea placeholder="Description (Supports multiline for bullets and **bold** text)" oninput="state.projects[${i}].desc=this.value; render()">${esc(item.desc)}</textarea>
    </div>`)
    .join("");
 
document.getElementById("tech-skill-fields").innerHTML = (currentTemplate === 'academic' || currentTemplate === 'innovative') && currentTemplate !== 'bordered' ? `
    <textarea
      id="in-techskills-academic"
      oninput="state.techSkills = this.value ? [{ cat: '', items: this.value }] : []; render();"
      placeholder="JavaScript, Python, React, Node.js, Docker..."
      style="width:100%; min-height: 78px;"
    >${esc(state.techSkills.length > 0 ? state.techSkills.map(ts => ts.items).join(', ') : '')}</textarea>
  ` : state.techSkills.map((item, i) => `
    <div class="dynamic-item">
      <button class="btn-del" onclick="remove('techSkills', ${i})" title="Remove">✕</button>
      <input placeholder="Category (e.g. Languages)" value="${esc(item.cat)}" oninput="state.techSkills[${i}].cat=this.value; render()" style="margin-bottom:8px">
      <input placeholder="Skills (e.g. C, C++, Python)" value="${esc(item.items)}" oninput="state.techSkills[${i}].items=this.value; render()">
    </div>`).join("");
 
  document.getElementById("achieve-fields").innerHTML = state.achievements
    .map((item, i) => {
      if (typeof item === 'string') {
        state.achievements[i] = { text: item, desc: '', link: '', linkText: '', linkType: 'separate' };
        item = state.achievements[i];
      }
      if (item.type !== undefined) {
        state.achievements[i] = { text: item.text || '', desc: item.desc || '', link: item.link || '', linkText: item.linkText || '', linkType: item.linkType || 'separate' };
        item = state.achievements[i];
      }
      if (!item.linkType) item.linkType = 'separate';
    return `
      <div class="dynamic-item">
        <button class="btn-del" onclick="remove('achievements', ${i})" title="Remove">✕</button>
        <input placeholder="Event / Achievement Name (supports **bold**)" value="${esc(item.text || '')}" oninput="state.achievements[${i}].text=this.value; render();" style="margin-bottom:8px;">
        ${currentTemplate !== 'academic' ? `<input placeholder="Date (e.g. Jan 2024)" value="${esc(item.date || '')}" oninput="state.achievements[${i}].date=this.value; render();" style="margin-bottom:8px;">` : ''}
        <textarea placeholder="Description (optional) — shown after a dash if filled" oninput="state.achievements[${i}].desc=this.value; render();" style="min-height:55px; margin-bottom:8px;">${esc(item.desc || '')}</textarea>
        <div class="form-grid">
          ${buildLinkTypeToggle('achievements', i, item.linkType)}
        </div>
        <div class="form-grid">
          ${buildLinkFields('achievements', i, item, 'https://...', 'e.g. Certificate, View')}
        </div>
      </div>`;
    }).join("");
 
  if (document.getElementById("cert-fields")) {
    document.getElementById("cert-fields").innerHTML = state.certifications
      .map((item, i) => {
        if (!item.linkType) item.linkType = 'separate';
        return `
        <div class="dynamic-item">
          <button class="btn-del" onclick="remove('certifications', ${i})" title="Remove">✕</button>
          <div class="form-grid" style="margin-bottom:8px">
            <input placeholder="Name / Title" value="${esc(item.name)}" oninput="state.certifications[${i}].name=this.value; render()">
            <input placeholder="${currentTemplate === 'attorney' ? 'Date (e.g. Jan 2024)' : 'Date / Details'}" value="${esc(item.date)}" oninput="state.certifications[${i}].date=this.value; render()">
          </div>
          <div class="form-grid">
            ${buildLinkTypeToggle('certifications', i, item.linkType)}
          </div>
          <div class="form-grid">
            ${buildLinkFields('certifications', i, item, 'Certificate Link (URL)', 'Link Label (clickable text)')}
          </div>
        </div>`;
      }).join("");
  }
 
  if (document.getElementById("extra-fields")) {
    document.getElementById("extra-fields").innerHTML = state.extracurricular
      .map((item, i) => {
        if (!item.linkType) item.linkType = 'separate';
        return `
        <div class="dynamic-item">
          <button class="btn-del" onclick="remove('extracurricular', ${i})" title="Remove">✕</button>
          <div class="form-grid" style="margin-bottom:8px">
            <input placeholder="Organization / Activity" value="${esc(item.org)}" oninput="state.extracurricular[${i}].org=this.value; render()">
            <input placeholder="Role (Optional)" value="${esc(item.role)}" oninput="state.extracurricular[${i}].role=this.value; render()">
          </div>
          ${currentTemplate !== 'academic' ? `
          <div class="form-grid" style="margin-bottom:8px">
            <input placeholder="Date" value="${esc(item.date)}" oninput="state.extracurricular[${i}].date=this.value; render()">
          </div>` : ''}
          <div class="label-row" style="margin-top:8px;"><label style="font-size:12px; color:#a094a0;">Description</label><button class="btn-ai" onclick="rewriteText(event, 'extracurricular', ${i})">✨ Enhance</button></div>
          <textarea placeholder="Brief description (shown after a dash)" oninput="state.extracurricular[${i}].desc=this.value; render()">${esc(item.desc)}</textarea>
          <div class="form-grid" style="margin-top: 10px;">
            ${buildLinkTypeToggle('extracurricular', i, item.linkType)}
          </div>
          <div class="form-grid">
            ${buildLinkFields('extracurricular', i, item, 'https://...', 'e.g. Event Page, Demo')}
          </div>
        </div>`;
      }).join("");
  }
 
  if (document.getElementById("skill-level-fields")) {
    document.getElementById("skill-level-fields").innerHTML = state.skillLevels.map((item, i) => `
      <div class="dynamic-item">
        <button class="btn-del" onclick="remove('skillLevels', ${i})" title="Remove">✕</button>
        <div class="form-grid">
          <input placeholder="Skill Name" value="${esc(item.name)}" oninput="state.skillLevels[${i}].name=this.value; render()">
          <input type="number" min="0" max="100" placeholder="Level % (0-100)" value="${esc(item.level)}" oninput="state.skillLevels[${i}].level=this.value; render()">
        </div>
      </div>
    `).join("");
  }
 
  // Sync link-display toggle buttons
  const liBtn = document.getElementById('linkedin-display-btn');
  if (liBtn) liBtn.textContent = (state.linkedinDisplay === 'url') ? 'URL' : 'Label';
  const ghBtn = document.getElementById('github-display-btn');
  if (ghBtn) ghBtn.textContent = (state.githubDisplay === 'url') ? 'URL' : 'Label';

  if (document.getElementById("reference-fields")) {
    document.getElementById("reference-fields").innerHTML = state.references.map((item, i) => `
      <div class="dynamic-item">
        <button class="btn-del" onclick="remove('references', ${i})" title="Remove">✕</button>
        <input placeholder="Reference Name" value="${esc(item.name)}" oninput="state.references[${i}].name=this.value; render()" style="margin-bottom:8px">
        <div class="form-grid">
          <input placeholder="Job Title" value="${esc(item.role)}" oninput="state.references[${i}].role=this.value; render()">
          <input placeholder="Company Name" value="${esc(item.company)}" oninput="state.references[${i}].company=this.value; render()">
        </div>
      </div>
    `).join("");
  }
}

      function buildAchievementLinkHtml(a, isAttorney) {
        if (!a.link || isTextLink(a)) return '';
        return buildSeparateLink(a, isAttorney, 'Link');
      }

      function buildAttorneyCertLink(c) {
        if (!c.link || isTextLink(c)) return '';
        const label = esc(c.linkText || c.link || 'Link');
        return ` <a href="${getUrl(c.link)}" class="pdf-link inline-link" target="_blank">${label}</a>`;
      }

      function applyTextLink(html, item, isAttorney) {
        if (!item.link || !isTextLink(item)) return html;
        const url = getUrl(item.link);
        return `<a href="${url}" target="_blank" style="display:inline; color:inherit; text-decoration:none; pointer-events:auto; position:relative; z-index:50;">${html}</a>`;
      }

    /* ── Bordered template helper — defined outside render() so it's always available ── */
    function bRows(items, labelHtml, makeContent, makeYear) {
      if (!items || items.length === 0) return '';
      return items.map((item, i) => {
        const isFirst = i === 0;
        const isLast  = i === items.length - 1;
        const noB = isFirst && !isLast ? ' no-bb' : (!isFirst && !isLast ? ' no-tb' : (isFirst ? '' : ' no-bt'));
        const labelCell = isFirst
          ? `<td rowspan="${items.length}" class="w-label" style="vertical-align:middle;">${labelHtml}</td>`
          : '';
        return `<tr>
          ${labelCell}
          <td class="w-content${noB}" style="vertical-align:top;">${makeContent(item, i)}</td>
          <td class="w-year${noB}">${makeYear(item, i)}</td>
        </tr>`;
      }).join('');
    }

    // --- RENDER PREVIEW ---
      function render() {
        normalizeState();
        
        const previewState = {};
        Object.keys(SAMPLE_DATA).forEach(k => {
          previewState[k] = state._touched[k] ? state[k] : SAMPLE_DATA[k];
        });
        previewState.template = state.template;

        (function(state) {
            const p = document.getElementById("preview");
            const isAnimating = p.classList.contains("animating");
            p.className = `resume-page tmpl-${state.template} ${isAnimating ? "animating" : ""}`;

            const skillArr = state.skills ? state.skills.split(",").map((s) => s.trim()).filter(Boolean) : [];
            const langArr = state.languages ? state.languages.split(",").map((s) => s.trim()).filter(Boolean) : [];
            const hobArr = state.hobbies ? state.hobbies.split(",").map((s) => s.trim()).filter(Boolean) : [];
            const cwArr = state.coursework ? state.coursework.split(",").map((s) => s.trim()).filter(Boolean) : [];

            const linkedinLabel = (state.linkedinDisplay === 'url' && state.linkedin) ? esc(state.linkedin) : 'LinkedIn';
            const githubLabel   = (state.githubDisplay  === 'url' && state.github)   ? esc(state.github)   : 'GitHub';

            const education = state.education;
            const experience = state.experience;
            const projects = state.projects;
            const techSkills = state.techSkills;
            const achievements = state.achievements;
            const certifications = state.certifications;
            const extracurricular = state.extracurricular;
            const skillLevels = state.skillLevels || [];
            const references = state.references || [];

        if (state.template === "academic") {
          p.innerHTML = `
            <div class="header-area">
              <div class="header-left">
                ${state.name ? `<h1 class="name-header">${esc(state.name)}</h1>` : ""}
                ${state.role ? `<div class="role-title">${esc(state.role)}</div>` : ""}
              </div>
              ${(state.phone || state.email || state.linkedin) ? `
              <div class="contact-area">
                 ${[
                  state.linkedin ? `<div style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:4px;">${icons.linkedin} <a href="${getUrl(state.linkedin)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank">${linkedinLabel}</a></div>` : "",
                   state.email ? `<div style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:4px;">${icons.email} <a href="mailto:${esc(state.email)}" class="pdf-link">${esc(state.email)}</a></div>` : "",
                   state.phone ? `<div style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:4px;">${icons.phone} ${esc(state.phone)}</div>` : ""
                 ].filter(Boolean).join("")}
              </div>
              ` : ""}
            </div>

            <div class="grid-container">
              <div class="left-col">
                ${state.summary ? `
                <h2>PROFILE</h2>
                <p>${formatText(state.summary)}</p>
                ` : ""}

                ${experience.length > 0 ? `
                <h2>EXPERIENCE</h2>
                ${experience.map(e => {
                  const titleHtml = applyTextLink(esc(e.title), e, false);
                  const sepLink = (!isTextLink(e) && e.link) ? buildSeparateLink(e, false, e.linkText || 'Link') : '';
                  return `
                  <div class="item-wrap">
                    <div class="item-title">${titleHtml}${sepLink}</div>
                    <div class="item-subtitle">${esc(e.company)}</div>
                    <div class="item-date">
                      ${icons.calendar}
                      ${esc(e.date)}
                    </div>
                    <ul>${formatDescToLi(e.desc)}</ul>
                  </div>`;
                }).join('')}
                ` : ""}

                ${projects.length > 0 ? `
                <h2>PROJECTS</h2>
                ${projects.map(proj => `
                  <div class="item-wrap">
                    <div class="item-title">${esc(proj.title)}</div>
                    ${proj.tech ? `<div class="item-subtitle">${esc(proj.tech)}</div>` : ''}
                    ${proj.date ? `
                    <div class="item-date">
                      ${icons.calendar}
                      ${esc(proj.date || '')}
                    </div>
                    ` : ''}
                    ${proj.link || proj.liveLink ? `
                    <div style="font-size: 8.5pt; margin-bottom: 4pt;">
                      ${proj.link ? `<a href="${getUrl(proj.link)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:#555;text-decoration:none;"><u>GitHub</u></a>` : ''}
                      ${proj.link && proj.liveLink ? ' | ' : ''}
                      ${proj.liveLink ? `<a href="${getUrl(proj.liveLink)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:#555;text-decoration:none;"><u>Live</u></a>` : ''}
                    </div>` : ''}
                    <ul>${formatDescToLi(proj.desc)}</ul>
                  </div>
                `).join('')}
                ` : ""}
              </div>

              <div class="right-col">
                ${skillArr.length > 0 ? `
                <h2>CORE SKILLS</h2>
                <div class="pill-container">
                  ${skillArr.map(s => `<div class="skill-pill">${esc(s)}</div>`).join('')}
                </div>
                ` : ""}

             ${techSkills.length > 0 ? `
                <h2>TECHNICAL SKILLS</h2>
                <div class="pill-container">
                  ${techSkills.map(ts => ts.items.split(',').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean).map(s => `<div class="skill-pill">${esc(s)}</div>`).join('')).join('')}
                </div>
                ` : ""}

                ${education.length > 0 ? `
                <h2>EDUCATION</h2>
                ${education.map(e => `
                  <div class="item-wrap" style="margin-bottom: 8pt;">
                    <div class="item-title" style="font-weight: 500;">${esc(e.degree)}</div>
                    <div class="item-subtitle" style="font-weight: 600;">${esc(e.school)}</div>
                    <div class="item-date" style="margin-top: 2pt;">
                      ${icons.calendar}
                      ${esc(e.date)}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                `).join('')}
                ` : ""}

                ${certifications.length > 0 ? `
                <h2>CERTIFICATIONS</h2>
                <ul class="clean-list">
                  ${certifications.map(c => {
                    const nameHtml = applyTextLink(esc(c.name), c, false);
                    const sepLink = (!isTextLink(c) && c.link) ? ` (<a href="${getUrl(c.link)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:#666; text-decoration:underline;">${esc(c.linkText || 'Link')}</a>)` : '';
                    return `<li>${nameHtml}${sepLink}${c.date ? ` <span style="color:#666; font-size:8pt;">(${esc(c.date)})</span>` : ''}</li>`;
                  }).join('')}
                </ul>
                ` : ""}

                ${hobArr.length > 0 ? `
                <h2>HOBBIES</h2>
                <ul class="clean-list">
                  ${hobArr.map(h => `<li>${esc(h)}</li>`).join('')}
                </ul>
                ` : ""}

                ${extracurricular.length > 0 ? `
                <h2>EXTRACURRICULAR</h2>
                <ul class="clean-list">
                  ${extracurricular.map(e => {
                    const orgHtml = applyTextLink(esc(e.org), e, false);
                    const sepLink = (!isTextLink(e) && e.link) ? buildSeparateLink(e, false, e.linkText || 'Link') : '';
                    const roleStr = e.role ? ` (${esc(e.role)})` : '';
                    const descStr = e.desc ? ` - ${formatText(e.desc)}` : '';
                    return `<li>${orgHtml}${roleStr}${descStr}${sepLink}</li>`;
                  }).join('')}
                </ul>
                ` : ""}

                ${achievements.length > 0 ? `
                <h2>ACHIEVEMENTS</h2>
                <ul class="clean-list">
                  ${achievements.map(a => {
                    if (typeof a === 'string') {
                      return a.split('\n').filter(l => l.trim()).map(line => `<li>${formatText(line)}</li>`).join('');
                    }
                    if (!a.linkType) a.linkType = 'separate';
                    const hasName = (a.text || '').trim().length > 0;
                    const hasDesc = (a.desc || '').trim().length > 0;
                    const linkHtml = buildAchievementLinkHtml(a, false);

                    if (hasName && hasDesc) {
                      const nameHtml = isTextLink(a) ? applyTextLink(`<strong>${formatText(a.text)}</strong>`, a, false) : `<strong>${formatText(a.text)}</strong>`;
                      return `<li>${nameHtml} \u2013 ${formatText(a.desc)}${linkHtml}</li>`;
                    } else if (hasName) {
                      if (isTextLink(a)) {
                        const lines = (a.text || '').split('\n').filter(l => l.trim());
                        return lines.map(line => `<li>${applyTextLink(formatText(line), a, false)}</li>`).join('');
                      }
                      const lines = (a.text || '').split('\n').filter(l => l.trim());
                      return lines.map((line, idx) => `<li>${formatText(line)}${idx === lines.length - 1 ? linkHtml : ''}</li>`).join('');
                    } else if (hasDesc) {
                      return `<li>${formatText(a.desc)}${linkHtml}</li>`;
                    }
                    return '';
                  }).join('')}
                </ul>
                ` : ""}
              </div>
            </div>
          `;

        } else if (state.template === "minimal") {
          p.innerHTML = `
            <div style="text-align: center; display: flex; flex-direction: column; align-items: center; gap: 4px; margin-bottom: 0;">
                <h1 class="resume-name" style="line-height: 0.75; margin: 0;">${esc(state.name)}</h1>
                ${state.address ? `<div style="font-size: 11.5pt; color: #000; line-height: 1; margin: 0;">${esc(state.address)}</div>` : ""}
                ${(state.phone || state.email || state.linkedin || state.github) ? `
                <div class="resume-contact-links" style="font-size: 10.5pt; display: flex; justify-content: center; align-items: center; gap: 14pt; flex-wrap: wrap; color: #000; margin: 0; line-height: 1;">
                  ${state.phone ? `<span style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:4px;">${icons.phone} <span class="contact-phone" style="position: relative; top: 1px;">${esc(state.phone)}</span></span>` : ""}
                  ${state.email ? `<span style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:4px;">${icons.email} <a href="mailto:${esc(state.email)}" class="pdf-link" style="color:#000; text-decoration:underline; text-underline-offset: 3px;">${esc(state.email)}</a></span>` : ""}
                  ${state.linkedin ? `<span style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:4px;">${icons.linkedin} <a href="${getUrl(state.linkedin)}" class="pdf-link" style="color:#000; text-decoration:underline; text-underline-offset: 3px;" target="_blank">${linkedinLabel}</a></span>` : ""}
${state.github ? `<span style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:4px;">${icons.github} <a href="${getUrl(state.github)}" class="pdf-link" style="color:#000; text-decoration:underline; text-underline-offset: 3px;" target="_blank">${githubLabel}</a></span>` : ""}
                </div>
                ` : ""}
            </div>

            ${state.summary ? `
            <div class="section-title">Professional Summary</div>
            <p>${formatText(state.summary)}</p>
            ` : ""}

            ${education.length > 0 ? `
            <div class="section-title">Education</div>
            ${education.map(e => `
              <div style="margin-bottom: 3pt;">
                <div class="flex-between" style="margin-bottom: 1pt;">
                  <div style="flex: 1; min-width: 0; max-width: 78%; padding-right: 15px;"><strong>${esc(e.school)}</strong></div>
                  <div style="white-space: nowrap; flex-shrink: 0; text-align: right;"><strong>${esc(e.date)}</strong></div>
                </div>
                <div class="flex-between">
                  <div style="flex: 1; min-width: 0; max-width: 78%; padding-right: 15px;"><em>${esc(e.degree)}</em></div>
                  <div style="white-space: nowrap; flex-shrink: 0; text-align: right;"><em>${esc(e.location)}</em></div>
                </div>
              </div>
            `).join('')}
            ` : ""}

            ${experience.length > 0 ? `
            <div class="section-title">Experience</div>
            ${experience.map(e => {
              const titleHtml = applyTextLink(`<strong>${esc(e.title)}</strong>`, e, false);
              const sepLink = (!isTextLink(e) && e.link) ? buildSeparateLink(e, false, e.linkText || 'Link') : '';
              return `
              <div style="margin-bottom: 4pt;">
                <div class="flex-between" style="margin-bottom: 1pt;">
                  <div style="flex: 1; min-width: 0; max-width: 78%; padding-right: 15px;">${titleHtml}${sepLink}</div>
                  <div style="white-space: nowrap; flex-shrink: 0; text-align: right;">${esc(e.date)}</div>
                </div>
                <div class="flex-between">
                  <div style="flex: 1; min-width: 0; max-width: 78%; padding-right: 15px;"><em>${esc(e.company)}</em></div>
                </div>
                <ul style="margin-top: 2pt;">${formatDescToLi(e.desc)}</ul>
              </div>`;
            }).join('')}
            ` : ""}

            ${cwArr.length > 0 ? `
            <div class="section-title">Relevant Coursework</div>
            <ul class="coursework-grid">
              ${cwArr.map(c => `<li>${esc(c)}</li>`).join('')}
            </ul>
            ` : ""}

            ${projects.length > 0 ? `
            <div class="section-title">Projects</div>
            ${projects.map(proj => `
              <div style="margin-bottom: 4pt;">
                <div class="flex-between" style="margin-bottom: 0pt;">
  <div style="flex: 1; min-width: 0; padding-right: 15px; display: flex; flex-wrap: wrap; align-items: baseline; gap: 0 4px;">
    <span style="display:inline; overflow-wrap:break-word; word-break:break-word;"><strong>${esc(proj.title)}</strong>${proj.tech ? `<span style="margin: 0 4px;">|</span><strong><em style="font-weight:700;">${esc(proj.tech)}</em></strong>` : ''}${proj.link ? `<span style="margin: 0 4px;">|</span><a href="${getUrl(proj.link)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:#000; text-decoration:underline; text-underline-offset: 3px;">GitHub</a>` : ''}${proj.liveLink ? `<span style="margin: 0 4px;">|</span><a href="${getUrl(proj.liveLink)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:#000; text-decoration:underline; text-underline-offset: 3px;">Live</a>` : ''}</span>
  </div>
  <div style="white-space: nowrap; flex-shrink: 0; text-align: right;">${esc(proj.date || '')}</div>
</div>
                <ul style="margin-top: 2pt;">${formatDescToLi(proj.desc)}</ul>
              </div>
            `).join('')}
            ` : ""}

            ${techSkills.length > 0 ? `
            <div class="section-title">Technical Skills</div>
            <div style="margin-bottom: 4pt;">
            ${techSkills.map(s => `
              <div style="margin-bottom: 1pt; margin-left: 16pt;">
                <strong>${esc(s.cat)}:</strong> ${esc(s.items)}
              </div>
            `).join('')}
            </div>
            ` : ""}

            ${certifications.length > 0 ? `
            <div class="section-title">Certifications</div>
            <ul>
            ${certifications.map(c => {
              const nameHtml = applyTextLink(esc(c.name), c, false);
              const sepLink = (!isTextLink(c) && c.link) ? ` <a href="${getUrl(c.link)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:#000; text-decoration:underline; text-underline-offset: 3px;">(${esc(c.linkText || 'Certificate')})</a>` : '';
              return `
              <li style="margin-bottom: 2pt;">
                <div class="flex-between">
                  <div style="flex: 1; min-width: 0; max-width: 78%; padding-right: 15px;">${nameHtml}${sepLink}</div>
                  <div style="white-space: nowrap; flex-shrink: 0; text-align: right;">${esc(c.date)}</div>
                </div>
              </li>`;
            }).join('')}
            </ul>
            ` : ""}

            ${extracurricular.length > 0 ? `
            <div class="section-title">Extracurricular</div>
            <ul>
            ${extracurricular.map(e => {
              const orgHtml = applyTextLink(`<strong>${esc(e.org)}</strong>`, e, false);
              const sepLink = (!isTextLink(e) && e.link) ? buildSeparateLink(e, false, e.linkText || 'Link') : '';
              return `
              <li style="margin-bottom: 2pt;">
                <div class="flex-between" style="margin-bottom: 2pt;">
                  <div style="flex: 1; min-width: 0; max-width: 78%; padding-right: 15px;">${orgHtml}${e.role ? ` — <em>${esc(e.role)}</em>` : ''}${sepLink}</div>
                  <div style="white-space: nowrap; flex-shrink: 0; text-align: right;">${esc(e.date)}</div>
                </div>
                ${e.desc ? `<ul style="margin-top: 2pt;">${formatDescToLi(e.desc)}</ul>` : ''}
              </li>`;
            }).join('')}
            </ul>
            ` : ""}

            ${achievements.length > 0 ? `
            <div class="section-title">Achievements</div>
            <ul>
              ${achievements.map(a => {
                if (typeof a === 'string') {
                  return `<li>${formatText(a)}</li>`;
                }
                if (!a.linkType) a.linkType = 'separate';
                const hasName = (a.text || '').trim().length > 0;
                const hasDesc = (a.desc || '').trim().length > 0;
                const linkHtml = buildAchievementLinkHtml(a, false);
                if (!hasName && !hasDesc) return '';

                if (hasName && hasDesc) {
                  const nameHtml = isTextLink(a) ? applyTextLink(`<strong>${formatText(a.text)}</strong>`, a, false) : `<strong>${formatText(a.text)}</strong>`;
                  return `<li>
                    <div class="flex-between">
                      <div style="flex:1; min-width:0; max-width:78%; padding-right:15px;">${nameHtml} \u2013 ${formatText(a.desc)}${linkHtml}</div>
                      <div style="white-space:nowrap; flex-shrink:0; text-align:right;">${esc(a.date || '')}</div>
                    </div>
                  </li>`;
                } else if (hasName) {
                  if (isTextLink(a)) {
                    const lines = (a.text || '').split('\n').filter(l => l.trim());
                    return lines.map((line, idx) => `<li>
                      <div class="flex-between">
                        <div style="flex:1; min-width:0; max-width:78%; padding-right:15px;">${applyTextLink(formatText(line), a, false)}</div>
                        ${idx === lines.length - 1 ? `<div style="white-space:nowrap; flex-shrink:0; text-align:right;">${esc(a.date || '')}</div>` : '<div></div>'}
                      </div>
                    </li>`).join('');
                  }
                  const lines = (a.text || '').split('\n').filter(l => l.trim());
                  return lines.map((line, idx) => `<li>
                    <div class="flex-between">
                      <div style="flex:1; min-width:0; max-width:78%; padding-right:15px;">${formatText(line)}${idx === lines.length - 1 ? linkHtml : ''}</div>
                      ${idx === lines.length - 1 ? `<div style="white-space:nowrap; flex-shrink:0; text-align:right;">${esc(a.date || '')}</div>` : '<div></div>'}
                    </div>
                  </li>`).join('');
                } else {
                  return `<li>
                    <div class="flex-between">
                      <div style="flex:1; min-width:0; max-width:78%; padding-right:15px;">${formatText(a.desc)}${linkHtml}</div>
                      <div style="white-space:nowrap; flex-shrink:0; text-align:right;">${esc(a.date || '')}</div>
                    </div>
                  </li>`;
                }
              }).join('')}
            </ul>
            ` : ""}
          `;

        } else if (state.template === "modern") {
          p.innerHTML = `
            <div class="sidebar" style="background: #292929; color: #e5e7eb; padding: 40pt 25pt;">
              ${state.photo ? `<img src="${state.photo}" class="pfp">` : ``}
              
              ${state.summary ? `
              <div class="sec-title-side">ABOUT ME</div>
              <div style="font-size: 9pt; line-height: 1.6; color: #ccc; margin-bottom: 30pt;">
                ${formatText(state.summary)}
              </div>` : ''}

              ${state.skillLevels && state.skillLevels.length > 0 ? `
              <div class="sec-title-side">SKILLS</div>
              <div class="side-timeline">
                ${state.skillLevels.map(s => `
                  <div class="side-item">
                    <div class="side-dot"></div>
                    <div style="font-size: 9pt; color: #fff; margin-bottom: 5pt; font-weight: 600;">${esc(s.name)}</div>
                    <div style="width: 100%; height: 4px; background: rgba(255,255,255,0.2);">
                      <div style="width: ${esc(s.level)}%; height: 100%; background: #fff;"></div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                `).join('')}
              </div>` : ''}

              ${state.references && state.references.length > 0 ? `
              <div class="sec-title-side">REFERENCE</div>
              <div class="side-timeline">
                ${state.references.map(r => `
                  <div class="side-item">
                    <div class="side-dot"></div>
                    <div style="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: 600; color: #fff; margin-bottom: 2pt;">${esc(r.name)}</div>
                    <div style="font-size: 8.5pt; color: #aaa; line-height: 1.4;">${esc(r.role)} | ${esc(r.company)}</div>
                  </div>
                `).join('')}
              </div>` : ''}

              ${hobArr.length > 0 || langArr.length > 0 ? `
              <div class="sec-title-side" style="margin-top: 30pt;">INTERESTS & LANGUAGES</div>
              <div style="font-size: 9pt; color: #ccc; line-height: 1.6;">
                ${langArr.length > 0 ? `<div style="margin-bottom: 6pt;"><strong>Languages:</strong> ${langArr.join(', ')}</div>` : ''}
                ${hobArr.length > 0 ? `<div><strong>Interests:</strong> ${hobArr.join(', ')}</div>` : ''}
              </div>
              ` : ''}
            </div>

            <div class="main">
              ${state.name ? `<h1 class="name-h1">${esc(state.name)}</h1>` : ""}
              ${state.role ? `<div class="role-h2">${esc(state.role)}</div>` : ""}

              ${(state.phone || state.email || state.address || state.linkedin || state.github) ? `
              <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; font-size: 9pt; color: #555; margin-bottom: 16pt; padding-right: 10pt;">
                <div>
                  ${state.phone ? `<div style="margin-bottom: 6pt;"><strong>P:</strong> ${esc(state.phone)}</div>` : ""}
                  ${state.email ? `<div><strong>E:</strong> <a href="mailto:${esc(state.email)}" class="pdf-link" style="color:inherit; text-decoration:none;">${esc(state.email)}</a></div>` : ""}
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: right;">
                  ${state.address ? `<div style="margin-bottom: 6pt;"><strong>A:</strong> ${esc(state.address)}</div>` : ""}
                 ${state.linkedin ? `<div style="margin-bottom: 6pt;"><strong>IN:</strong> <a href="${getUrl(state.linkedin)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:inherit; text-decoration:none;">${linkedinLabel}</a></div>` : ""}
${state.github ? `<div><strong>GH:</strong> <a href="${getUrl(state.github)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:inherit; text-decoration:none;">${githubLabel}</a></div>` : ""}
                </div>
              </div>
              ` : ""}

              ${experience.length > 0 ? `
              <div class="sec-title-main">WORK EXPERIENCE</div>
              <div class="timeline">
                ${experience.map(e => {
                  const titleHtml = applyTextLink(esc(e.title), e, false);
                  const sepLink = (!isTextLink(e) && e.link) ? buildSeparateLink(e, false, e.linkText || 'Link') : '';
                  return `
                  <div class="timeline-item">
                    <div class="timeline-dot"></div>
                    <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: baseline; margin-bottom: 4pt;">
                      <div style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: 600; flex: 1; min-width: 0; padding-right: 15px;">${titleHtml}${sepLink}</div>
                      <div style="font-size: 8.5pt; color: #777; white-space: nowrap; flex-shrink: 0;">${esc(e.date)}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div style="font-size: 9.5pt; color: #555; margin-bottom: 6pt;">${esc(e.company)}</div>
                    <ul class="bullets">${formatDescToLi(e.desc)}</ul>
                  </div>`;
                }).join('')}
              </div>` : ""}

              ${education.length > 0 ? `
              <div class="sec-title-main">EDUCATION</div>
              <div class="timeline">
                ${education.map(e => `
                  <div class="timeline-item">
                    <div class="timeline-dot"></div>
                    <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: baseline; margin-bottom: 4pt;">
                      <div style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: 600; flex: 1; min-width: 0; padding-right: 15px;">${esc(e.school)}</div>
                      <div style="font-size: 8.5pt; color: #777; white-space: nowrap; flex-shrink: 0;">${esc(e.date)}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div style="font-size: 9.5pt; color: #555;">${esc(e.degree)}${e.location ? ` — ${esc(e.location)}` : ''}</div>
                  </div>
                `).join('')}
              </div>` : ""}

              ${projects.length > 0 ? `
              <div class="sec-title-main">PROJECTS</div>
              <div class="timeline">
                ${projects.map(proj => `
                  <div class="timeline-item">
                    <div class="timeline-dot"></div>
                    <div style="display: flex; flex-wrap: wrap; align-items: baseline; margin-bottom: 4pt; gap: 0 8pt;">
  <div style="font-size: 12pt; font-weight: 600; white-space: nowrap; flex-shrink: 0;">${esc(proj.title)}</div>
  ${proj.tech ? `<div style="font-size: 8.5pt; color: #777; overflow-wrap: break-word; word-break: break-word; flex: 1; min-width: 0;">${esc(proj.tech)}</div>` : ''}
  ${proj.date ? `<div style="font-size: 8.5pt; color: #777; white-space: nowrap; flex-shrink: 0;">${esc(proj.date)}</div>` : ''}
</div>
                    <ul class="bullets">${formatDescToLi(proj.desc)}</ul>
                  </div>
                `).join('')}
              </div>` : ""}
            </div>
          `;

        } else if (state.template === "attorney") {
          p.innerHTML = `
            <div class="name">${esc(state.name)}</div>

            ${(state.phone || state.email || state.linkedin || state.github) ? `
            <div class="contact">
              ${[
                state.phone ? esc(state.phone) : '',
                state.email ? `<a href="mailto:${esc(state.email)}" class="pdf-link">${esc(state.email)}</a>` : '',
              state.linkedin ? `<a href="${getUrl(state.linkedin)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank">${linkedinLabel}</a>` : '',
state.github ? `<a href="${getUrl(state.github)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank">${githubLabel}</a>` : ''
              ].filter(Boolean).join(" | ")}
            </div>
            ` : ""}

            ${state.summary ? `
            <section class="section">
                <div class="section-title">Summary</div>
                <div class="summary-text">${formatText(state.summary)}</div>
            </section>
            ` : ""}

            ${education.length > 0 ? `
            <section class="section">
                <div class="section-title">Education</div>
                <div class="entry indent">
                ${education.map((e, index) => `
                    <div class="topline" ${index > 0 ? 'style="margin-top: 4px;"' : ''}>
                        <div class="left-block institution">${esc(e.school)}</div>
                        <div class="right-block body-text">${esc(e.date)}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="subline">
                        <div class="left">${esc(e.degree)}</div>
                        <div class="right">${esc(e.location)}</div>
                    </div>
                `).join('')}
                </div>
            </section>
            ` : ""}

            ${experience.length > 0 ? `
            <section class="section">
                <div class="section-title">Experience</div>
                ${experience.map((e, index) => {
                  const titleHtml = applyTextLink(esc(e.title), e, true);
                  const sepLink = (!isTextLink(e) && e.link) ? buildSeparateLink(e, true, e.linkText || 'Link') : '';
                  return `
                  <div class="entry indent" ${index > 0 ? 'style="margin-top: 14px;"' : ''}>
                      <div class="topline">
                          <div class="left-block role">${titleHtml}${sepLink}</div>
                          <div class="right-block body-text">${esc(e.date)}</div>
                      </div>
                      <div class="subline">
                          <div class="left">${esc(e.company)}</div>
                          <div class="right">${esc(e.location || '')}</div>
                      </div>
                      <ul class="details">
                          ${formatDescToLi(e.desc)}
                      </ul>
                  </div>`;
                }).join('')}
            </section>
            ` : ""}

            ${projects.length > 0 ? `
            <section class="section">
                <div class="section-title">Projects</div>
                ${projects.map((proj, index) => `
                <div class="entry indent" ${index > 0 ? 'style="margin-top: 14px;"' : ''}>
                    <div class="topline">
                       <div class="left-block" style="font-size: 14px;">
                            <span class="project-name">${esc(proj.title)}</span>
                            ${proj.tech ? `<span> | </span><span class="tech-stack">${esc(proj.tech)}</span>` : ''}
                            ${proj.link ? `<span> | </span><a href="${getUrl(proj.link)}" class="pdf-link inline-link" target="_blank">GitHub</a>` : ''}
                            ${proj.liveLink ? `<span> | </span><a href="${getUrl(proj.liveLink)}" class="pdf-link inline-link" target="_blank">Demo</a>` : ''}
                        </div>
                        <div class="right-block body-text">${esc(proj.date || '')}</div>
                    </div>
                    <ul class="details">
                        ${formatDescToLi(proj.desc)}
                    </ul>
                </div>
                `).join('')}
            </section>
            ` : ""}

            ${certifications.length > 0 ? `
            <section class="section">
                <div class="section-title">Hackathons &amp; Competitive Programming</div>
                <div class="entry indent">
                ${certifications.map((c, index) => {
                  if (!c.linkType) c.linkType = 'separate';
                  const nameHtml = isTextLink(c) ? applyTextLink(`<span class="hack-title">${formatText(c.name)}</span>`, c, true) : `<span class="hack-title">${formatText(c.name)}</span>`;
                  const sepLink = (!isTextLink(c) && c.link) ? buildAttorneyCertLink(c) : '';
                  return `
                  <div class="hack-line" ${index > 0 ? 'style="margin-top: 8px;"' : ''}>
                      <span class="hack-title">${nameHtml}</span>
                      ${c.date ? `<span> \u2014 ${formatText(c.date)}</span>` : ''}
                      ${sepLink}
                  </div>`;
                }).join('')}
                </div>
            </section>
            ` : ""}

            ${techSkills.length > 0 ? `
            <section class="section">
                <div class="section-title">Technical Skills</div>
                <div class="entry indent">
                ${techSkills.map((s, index) => `
                    <div class="skill-line" ${index > 0 ? 'style="margin-top: 5.25px;"' : ''}><span class="skill-label">${esc(s.cat)}:</span> ${esc(s.items)}</div>
                `).join('')}
                </div>
            </section>
            ` : ""}

            ${(extracurricular.length > 0 || achievements.length > 0) ? `
            <section class="section">
                <div class="section-title">Leadership &amp; Achievements</div>
                <div class="entry indent">
                ${extracurricular.map((e, index) => {
                  if (!e.linkType) e.linkType = 'separate';
                  const orgStr = e.org + (e.date ? ` (${e.date})` : '');
                  const orgHtml = isTextLink(e) ? applyTextLink(`<span class="achievement-strong">${esc(orgStr)}</span>`, e, true) : `<span class="achievement-strong">${esc(orgStr)}</span>`;
                  const sepLink = (!isTextLink(e) && e.link) ? buildSeparateLink(e, true, e.linkText || 'Link') : '';
                 return `
                  <div class="achievement-line" ${index > 0 ? 'style="margin-top: 8px;"' : ''}>
                      ${orgHtml}${e.role ? ` \u2013 ${esc(e.role)}` : ''}${e.desc ? ' ' + e.desc.replace(/\*\*/g, '').replace(/\n/g, ' ') : ''}${sepLink}
                  </div>`;
                }).join('')}
                ${achievements.map((a, index) => {
                  if (!a.linkType) a.linkType = 'separate';
                  const isFirst = index === 0 && extracurricular.length === 0;
                  const marginStyle = (!isFirst) ? 'style="margin-top: 5.25px;"' : '';

                  if (typeof a === 'string') {
                    return a.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim()).map((line, subIndex) => {
                      let cleaned = formatText(line).replace(/^[•–—*\-]\s*/ , '');
                      return `<div class="achievement-line" ${(index > 0 || extracurricular.length > 0 || subIndex > 0) ? 'style="margin-top: 5.25px;"' : ''}>${cleaned.replace(/<strong>/g, '<span class="achievement-strong">').replace(/<\/strong>/g, '</span>')}</div>`;
                    }).join('');
                  }

                  const hasName = (a.text || '').trim().length > 0;
                  const hasDesc = (a.desc || '').trim().length > 0;
                  const linkHtml = buildAchievementLinkHtml(a, true);

                  if (hasName && hasDesc) {
                    let nameFormatted = formatText(a.text).replace(/<strong>/g, '<span class="achievement-strong">').replace(/<\/strong>/g, '</span>');
                    const nameHtml = isTextLink(a) ? applyTextLink(`<span class="achievement-strong">${nameFormatted}</span>`, a, true) : `<span class="achievement-strong">${nameFormatted}</span>`;
                    const dateHtml = a.date ? ` <span style="font-weight:700; font-style:normal;">(${esc(a.date)})</span>` : '';
                    return `<div class="achievement-line" ${(index > 0 || extracurricular.length > 0) ? 'style="margin-top: 8px;"' : ''}>${nameHtml}${dateHtml} \u2013 ${formatText(a.desc)}${linkHtml}</div>`;
                  } else {
                    const t = (a.text || a.desc || '');
                    if (isTextLink(a) && t.trim()) {
                      const firstLine = t.split('\n').filter(l => l.trim())[0] || '';
                      const rest = t.split('\n').filter(l => l.trim()).slice(1);
                      let html = `<div class="achievement-line" ${(index > 0 || extracurricular.length > 0) ? 'style="margin-top: 5.25px;"' : ''}>${applyTextLink(formatText(firstLine.replace(/^[•–—*\-]\s*/ , '')), a, true)}</div>`;
                      rest.forEach((line) => {
                        let cleaned = formatText(line).replace(/^[•–—*\-]\s*/ , '');
                        html += `<div class="achievement-line" style="margin-top: 5.25px;">${cleaned}</div>`;
                      });
                      return html;
                    }
                   return t.split('\n').filter(line => line.trim()).map((line, subIndex) => {
                      let cleaned = formatText(line).replace(/^[•–—*\-]\s*/ , '');
                      const isLast = subIndex === t.split('\n').filter(l => l.trim()).length - 1;
                      const dateHtml = (isLast && a.date) ? ` <span style="font-weight:700; font-style:normal;">(${esc(a.date)})</span>` : '';
                      return `<div class="achievement-line" ${(index > 0 || extracurricular.length > 0 || subIndex > 0) ? 'style="margin-top: 5.25px;"' : ''}>${cleaned.replace(/<strong>/g, '<span class="achievement-strong">').replace(/<\/strong>/g, '</span>')}${dateHtml}${isLast ? linkHtml : ''}</div>`;
                    }).join('');
                  }
                }).join('')}
                </div>
            </section>
            ` : ""}
          `;

        } else if (state.template === "bordered") {

          p.innerHTML = `
            ${state.tagline ? `<div class="b-header"><b>${esc(state.tagline)}</b></div>` : ''}

            <!-- PERSONAL INFO / CONTACT -->
            <table>
              <tr>
                <th colspan="5" class="b-sec">PERSONAL INFORMATION</th>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td style="width:20%; text-align:center;"><b>Name</b></td>
                <td style="width:30%; text-align:center;">${esc(state.name)}</td>
                <td style="width:20%; text-align:center;"><b>Email</b></td>
                <td style="width:25%; text-align:center;">${state.email ? `<a href="mailto:${esc(state.email)}" style="color:#000;">${esc(state.email)}</a>` : ''}</td>
                <td style="width:5%;"></td>
              </tr>
              ${(state.phone || state.linkedin || state.address) ? `<tr>
                <td style="text-align:center;"><b>Phone</b></td>
                <td style="text-align:center;">${esc(state.phone)}</td>
                <td style="text-align:center;"><b>${state.linkedin ? 'LinkedIn' : (state.address ? 'Location' : '')}</b></td>
                <td style="text-align:center;">${state.linkedin ? `<a href="${getUrl(state.linkedin)}" target="_blank" style="color:#000;">${esc(state.linkedin)}</a>` : esc(state.address)}</td>
                <td></td>
              </tr>` : ''}
              ${state.github ? `<tr>
                <td style="text-align:center;"><b>GitHub</b></td>
                <td colspan="3" style="text-align:center;"><a href="${getUrl(state.github)}" target="_blank" style="color:#000;">${esc(state.github)}</a></td>
                <td></td>
              </tr>` : ''}
              ${state.summary ? `<tr>
                <td style="text-align:center;"><b>Summary</b></td>
                <td colspan="3" style="text-align:justify;">${formatText(state.summary)}</td>
                <td></td>
              </tr>` : ''}
            </table>

            <!-- EDUCATION -->
            ${education.length > 0 ? `
            <table>
              <tr><th colspan="5" class="b-sec">EDUCATION</th></tr>
              ${education.map(e => `<tr>
                <td style="width:16%; text-align:center;">${esc(e.degree)}</td>
                <td style="width:34%; text-align:center;">${esc(e.school)}</td>
                <td style="width:10%; text-align:center;">${e.location ? `<b>${esc(e.location)}</b>` : ''}</td>
                <td style="width:35%; text-align:center;">${e.gpa ? `<b>${esc(e.gpa)}</b>` : ''}</td>
                <td style="width:5%; text-align:center;">${esc(e.date)}</td>
              </tr>`).join('')}
            </table>` : ''}

            <!-- ACADEMIC / REGULAR ACHIEVEMENTS -->
            ${achievements.length > 0 ? `
            <table>
              <tr><th colspan="3" class="b-sec">ACHIEVEMENTS</th></tr>
              ${bRows(achievements,
                '',
                (a) => `<ul><li>${formatText(a.text || '')}${a.desc ? ' \u2013 ' + formatText(a.desc) : ''}${buildAchievementLinkHtml(a, false)}</li></ul>`,
                (a) => esc(a.date || '')
              )}
            </table>` : ''}

            <!-- WORK EXPERIENCE -->
            ${experience.length > 0 ? `
            <table>
              <tr><th colspan="3" class="b-sec">WORK EXPERIENCE</th></tr>
              ${experience.map((e, i) => {
                const isFirst = i === 0;
                const isLast  = i === experience.length - 1;
                const noB = isFirst && !isLast ? ' no-bb' : (!isFirst && !isLast ? ' no-tb' : (isFirst ? '' : ' no-bt'));
                const titleHtml = applyTextLink(esc(e.title), e, false);
                const sepLink = (!isTextLink(e) && e.link) ? buildSeparateLink(e, false, e.linkText || 'Link') : '';
                return `<tr>
                  <td class="w-label${noB}" style="text-align:center;"><b>${titleHtml}</b><br><span style="font-weight:normal;">${esc(e.company)}</span></td>
                  <td class="w-content${noB}" style="vertical-align:top;">
                    <ul>${formatDescToLi(e.desc)}</ul>${sepLink}
                  </td>
                  <td class="w-year${noB}">${esc(e.date)}</td>
                </tr>`;
              }).join('')}
            </table>` : ''}

            <!-- PROJECTS -->
            ${projects.length > 0 ? `
            <table>
              <tr><th colspan="3" class="b-sec">PROJECTS</th></tr>
              ${projects.map((proj, i) => {
                const isFirst = i === 0;
                const isLast  = i === projects.length - 1;
                const noB = isFirst && !isLast ? ' no-bb' : (!isFirst && !isLast ? ' no-tb' : (isFirst ? '' : ' no-bt'));
                return `<tr>
                  <td class="w-label${noB}" style="text-align:center;"><b>${esc(proj.title)}</b>${proj.tech ? `<br><span style="font-weight:normal;font-size:10px;">${esc(proj.tech)}</span>` : ''}</td>
                  <td class="w-content${noB}" style="vertical-align:top;">
                    <ul>${formatDescToLi(proj.desc)}</ul>
                    ${(proj.link || proj.liveLink) ? `<div style="font-size:10px; margin-top:2px;">${proj.link ? `<a href="${getUrl(proj.link)}" target="_blank" style="color:#000;"><u>GitHub</u></a>` : ''}${proj.link && proj.liveLink ? ' | ' : ''}${proj.liveLink ? `<a href="${getUrl(proj.liveLink)}" target="_blank" style="color:#000;"><u>Live</u></a>` : ''}</div>` : ''}
                  </td>
                  <td class="w-year${noB}">${esc(proj.date || '')}</td>
                </tr>`;
              }).join('')}
            </table>` : ''}

            <!-- CERTIFICATIONS -->
            ${certifications.length > 0 ? `
            <table>
              <tr><th colspan="3" class="b-sec">CERTIFICATIONS</th></tr>
              ${bRows(certifications,
                '<b>Certifications</b>',
                (c) => { const nH = applyTextLink(esc(c.name), c, false); const sL = (!isTextLink(c) && c.link) ? buildSeparateLink(c, false, c.linkText || 'Certificate') : ''; return `<ul><li>${nH}${sL}</li></ul>`; },
                (c) => esc(c.date || '')
              )}
            </table>` : ''}

            <!-- TECHNICAL SKILLS -->
            ${techSkills.length > 0 ? `
            <table>
              <tr><th colspan="3" class="b-sec">TECHNICAL SKILLS</th></tr>
              ${techSkills.map((ts, i) => {
                const isFirst = i === 0;
                const isLast  = i === techSkills.length - 1;
                const noB = isFirst && !isLast ? ' no-bb' : (!isFirst && !isLast ? ' no-tb' : (isFirst ? '' : ' no-bt'));
                return `<tr>
                  <td class="w-label${noB}" style="text-align:center;"><b>${esc(ts.cat)}</b></td>
                  <td class="w-content${noB}">${esc(ts.items)}</td>
                  <td class="w-year${noB}"></td>
                </tr>`;
              }).join('')}
            </table>` : ''}

            <!-- EXTRACURRICULAR / POSITIONS OF RESPONSIBILITY -->
            ${extracurricular.length > 0 ? `
            <table>
              <tr><th colspan="4" class="b-sec">POSITIONS OF RESPONSIBILITY / EXTRA-CURRICULAR</th></tr>
              ${extracurricular.map((e) => {
                const orgHtml = applyTextLink(esc(e.org), e, false);
                const sepLink = (!isTextLink(e) && e.link) ? buildSeparateLink(e, false, e.linkText || 'Link') : '';
                return `<tr>
                  <td class="vert-col" style="width:3%;"><div class="vert-text">${esc(e.org).substring(0,6).toUpperCase()}</div></td>
                  <td class="role-col" style="text-align:center;"><b>${esc(e.role || 'Member')}</b></td>
                  <td class="w-content" style="vertical-align:top;">
                    <ul>${formatDescToLi(e.desc)}</ul>${sepLink}
                  </td>
                  <td class="w-year">${esc(e.date || '')}</td>
                </tr>`;
              }).join('')}
            </table>` : ''}

            <!-- SKILLS + HOBBIES -->
            ${(skillArr.length > 0 || hobArr.length > 0 || langArr.length > 0) ? `
            <table>
              <tr><th colspan="3" class="b-sec">SKILLS &amp; INTERESTS</th></tr>
              ${skillArr.length > 0 ? `<tr>
                <td class="w-label${hobArr.length > 0 || langArr.length > 0 ? ' no-bb' : ''}" style="text-align:center;"><b>Core Skills</b></td>
                <td class="w-content${hobArr.length > 0 || langArr.length > 0 ? ' no-bb' : ''}">${skillArr.map(s=>`<span style="display:inline-block;border:1px solid #ccc;border-radius:2px;padding:1px 5px;margin:1px;font-size:10px;">${esc(s)}</span>`).join(' ')}</td>
                <td class="w-year${hobArr.length > 0 || langArr.length > 0 ? ' no-bb' : ''}"></td>
              </tr>` : ''}
              ${langArr.length > 0 ? `<tr>
                <td class="w-label${hobArr.length > 0 ? ' no-tb' : ' no-bt'}" style="text-align:center;"><b>Languages</b></td>
                <td class="w-content${hobArr.length > 0 ? ' no-tb' : ' no-bt'}">${langArr.join(', ')}</td>
                <td class="w-year${hobArr.length > 0 ? ' no-tb' : ' no-bt'}"></td>
              </tr>` : ''}
              ${hobArr.length > 0 ? `<tr>
                <td class="w-label${skillArr.length > 0 || langArr.length > 0 ? ' no-bt' : ''}" style="text-align:center;"><b>Interests</b></td>
                <td class="w-content${skillArr.length > 0 || langArr.length > 0 ? ' no-bt' : ''}">${hobArr.join(', ')}</td>
                <td class="w-year${skillArr.length > 0 || langArr.length > 0 ? ' no-bt' : ''}"></td>
              </tr>` : ''}
            </table>` : ''}
          `;

        } else if (state.template === "innovative") {
          p.innerHTML = `
            <div class="header" style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; margin-bottom: 12pt; border-bottom: 1px solid #e5e7eb; padding-bottom: 10pt;">
              <div class="header-info" style="flex: 1;">
                ${state.name ? '<div class="name" style="font-size: 26pt; font-weight: 800; color: #1e3a8a; text-transform: uppercase; letter-spacing: 0.5px; line-height: 1; margin-bottom: 3pt;">' + esc(state.name) + '</div>' : ''}
                ${state.role ? '<div class="role" style="font-size: 11pt; color: #3b82f6; font-weight: 600; margin-bottom: 6pt;">' + esc(state.role) + '</div>' : ''}
                <div class="contact-info" style="display: flex; gap: 10pt; font-size: 8pt; color: #555; flex-wrap: wrap;">
                  ${state.email ? '<span style="display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 4px;">' + icons.email + '<a href="mailto:' + esc(state.email) + '" class="pdf-link" style="color:inherit;text-decoration:none;">' + esc(state.email) + '</a></span>' : ''}
                  ${state.phone ? '<span style="display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 4px;">' + icons.phone + esc(state.phone) + '</span>' : ''}
                 ${state.linkedin ? '<span style="display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 4px;">' + icons.linkedin + '<a href="' + getUrl(state.linkedin) + '" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:inherit;text-decoration:none;">' + linkedinLabel + '</a></span>' : ''}
${state.github ? '<span style="display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 4px;">' + icons.github + '<a href="' + getUrl(state.github) + '" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:inherit;text-decoration:none;">' + githubLabel + '</a></span>' : ''}
                  ${state.address ? '<span style="display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 4px;">' + icons.pin + esc(state.address) + '</span>' : ''}
                </div>
              </div>
              ${state.photo ? '<div class="pfp-container" style="width: 80px; height: 80px; border-radius: 50%; overflow: hidden; flex-shrink: 0; margin-left: 15pt;"><img src="' + state.photo + '" class="pfp" style="width: 100%; height: 100%; object-fit: cover;"></div>' : ''}
            </div>

            <div class="body-grid" style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: 60% 35%; gap: 5%;">
              <div class="left-col">
                ${state.summary ? `
                  <div class="section-title" style="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: 700; color: #71717a; text-transform: uppercase; border-bottom: 1px solid #e5e7eb; padding-bottom: 2pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; letter-spacing: 0.5px;">SUMMARY</div>
                  <div class="desc" style="font-size: 8.5pt; color: #4b5563; line-height: 1.35; margin-bottom: 12pt; text-align: justify;">${formatText(state.summary)}</div>
                ` : ""}

                ${experience.length > 0 ? `
                  <div class="section-title" style="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: 700; color: #71717a; text-transform: uppercase; border-bottom: 1px solid #e5e7eb; padding-bottom: 2pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; letter-spacing: 0.5px;">EXPERIENCE</div>
                  ${experience.map(e => {
                    const titleHtml = applyTextLink(esc(e.title), e, false);
                    const sepLink = (!isTextLink(e) && e.link) ? buildSeparateLink(e, false, e.linkText || 'Link') : '';
                    return `
                    <div class="item" style="margin-bottom: 8pt;">
                      <div class="item-header" style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: baseline; margin-bottom: 1pt;">
                        <div class="item-title" style="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: 700; color: #1e3a8a;">${titleHtml}${sepLink}</div>
                        <div class="item-date" style="font-size: 8pt; color: #71717a; font-weight: 500;">${esc(e.date)}</div>
                      </div>
                      <div class="item-subtitle" style="font-size: 9pt; color: #3b82f6; font-weight: 500; margin-bottom: 2pt;">${esc(e.company)}</div>
                      <ul class="desc-list" style="margin: 0; padding-left: 12pt; font-size: 8.5pt; color: #4b5563; line-height: 1.35;">${formatDescToLi(e.desc)}</ul>
                    </div>`;
                  }).join('')}
                ` : ""}

                ${education.length > 0 ? `
                  <div class="section-title" style="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: 700; color: #71717a; text-transform: uppercase; border-bottom: 1px solid #e5e7eb; padding-bottom: 2pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; letter-spacing: 0.5px;">EDUCATION</div>
                  ${education.map(e => `
                    <div class="item" style="margin-bottom: 8pt;">
                      <div class="item-header" style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: baseline; margin-bottom: 1pt;">
                       <div class="item-title" style="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: 700; color: #1e3a8a;">${esc(e.school)}</div>
                        <div class="item-date" style="font-size: 8pt; color: #71717a; font-weight: 500;">${esc(e.date)}</div>
                      </div>
                      <div class="item-subtitle" style="font-size: 9pt; color: #3b82f6; font-weight: 500; margin-bottom: 2pt;">${esc(e.degree)}</div>
                      <div class="desc" style="font-size: 8.5pt; color: #4b5563; line-height: 1.35;">${esc(e.location)}</div>
                    </div>
                  `).join('')}
                ` : ""}

                ${projects.length > 0 ? `
                  <div class="section-title" style="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: 700; color: #71717a; text-transform: uppercase; border-bottom: 1px solid #e5e7eb; padding-bottom: 2pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; letter-spacing: 0.5px;">PROJECTS</div>
                  ${projects.map(proj => `
                    <div class="item" style="margin-bottom: 8pt;">
                      <div class="item-header" style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: baseline; margin-bottom: 1pt;">
                        <div class="item-title" style="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: 700; color: #1e3a8a;">${esc(proj.title)}</div>
                        <div class="item-date" style="font-size: 8pt; color: #71717a; font-weight: 500;">${esc(proj.date || '')}</div>
                      </div>
                      <div class="item-subtitle" style="font-size: 9pt; color: #3b82f6; font-weight: 500; margin-bottom: 2pt;">
                        ${esc(proj.tech)}
                        ${proj.link ? ` | <a href="${getUrl(proj.link)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:inherit;">GitHub</a>` : ''}
                        ${proj.liveLink ? ` | <a href="${getUrl(proj.liveLink)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:inherit;">Live</a>` : ''}
                      </div>
                      <ul class="desc-list" style="margin: 0; padding-left: 12pt; font-size: 8.5pt; color: #4b5563; line-height: 1.35;">${formatDescToLi(proj.desc)}</ul>
                    </div>
                  `).join('')}
                ` : ""}
              </div>

              <div class="right-col">
              ${techSkills.length > 0 ? `
                  <div class="section-title" style="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: 700; color: #71717a; text-transform: uppercase; border-bottom: 1px solid #e5e7eb; padding-bottom: 2pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; letter-spacing: 0.5px;">SKILLS</div>
                  <div style="margin-bottom: 12pt;">
                    ${techSkills.map(ts => ts.items.split(',').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean).map(s => `<span class="skill-item" style="display: inline-block; font-size: 8pt; background: #eff6ff; padding: 2pt 6pt; border-radius: 4px; margin: 0 4pt 4pt 0; color: #1e3a8a; font-weight: 500;">${esc(s)}</span>`).join('')).join('')}
                  </div>
                ` : ""}

                ${achievements.length > 0 ? `
                  <div class="section-title" style="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: 700; color: #71717a; text-transform: uppercase; border-bottom: 1px solid #e5e7eb; padding-bottom: 2pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; letter-spacing: 0.5px;">ACHIEVEMENTS</div>
                  <div style="margin-bottom: 12pt;">
                 ${achievements.map((a) => {
                    if (!a.linkType) a.linkType = 'separate';
                    if (typeof a === 'string') {
                      let lines = a.split('\n').filter(l=>l.trim());
                      return lines.map((line) => {
                        let iconSvg = '<svg width="10" height="10" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path d="M12 2l3.09 6.26L22 9.27l-5 4.87 1.18 6.88L12 17.77l-6.18 3.25L7 14.14 2 9.27l6.91-1.01L12 2z"></path></svg>';
                        return '<div class="achievement-block" style="display: flex; gap: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; align-items: flex-start;">' +
                                 '<div class="ach-icon" style="width: 20px; height: 20px; background: #eff6ff; border-radius: 50%; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center; color: #3b82f6; flex-shrink: 0; margin-top: 1px;">' + iconSvg + '</div>' +
                                 '<div class="ach-content" style="flex: 1;"><div class="desc" style="font-size: 8.5pt; color: #4b5563; line-height: 1.35;">' + formatText(line.replace(/^[•–—*\-]\s*/ , '')) + '</div></div>' +
                               '</div>';
                      }).join('');
                    }
                    const linkHtml = buildAchievementLinkHtml(a, false);
                    const hasName = (a.text || '').trim().length > 0;
                    const hasDesc = (a.desc || '').trim().length > 0;
                    let iconSvg = '<svg width="10" height="10" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path d="M12 2l3.09 6.26L22 9.27l-5 4.87 1.18 6.88L12 17.77l-6.18 3.25L7 14.14 2 9.27l6.91-1.01L12 2z"></path></svg>';
                    if (hasName && hasDesc) {
                      const nameHtml = isTextLink(a) ? applyTextLink(`<strong>${formatText(a.text)}</strong>`, a, false) : `<strong>${formatText(a.text)}</strong>`;
                      let content = `${nameHtml} \u2013 ${formatText(a.desc)}${linkHtml}`;
                      return '<div class="achievement-block" style="display: flex; gap: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; align-items: flex-start;">' +
                               '<div class="ach-icon" style="width: 20px; height: 20px; background: #eff6ff; border-radius: 50%; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center; color: #3b82f6; flex-shrink: 0; margin-top: 1px;">' + iconSvg + '</div>' +
                               '<div class="ach-content" style="flex: 1;"><div class="desc" style="font-size: 8.5pt; color: #4b5563; line-height: 1.35;">' + content + '</div></div>' +
                             '</div>';
                    } else {
                      const t = a.text || a.desc || '';
                      return t.split('\n').filter(l=>l.trim()).map((line, idx, arr) => {
                        const isLast = idx === arr.length - 1;
                        const lineHtml = isTextLink(a) ? applyTextLink(formatText(line.replace(/^[•–—*\-]\s*/ , '')), a, false) : formatText(line.replace(/^[•–—*\-]\s*/ , ''));
                        return '<div class="achievement-block" style="display: flex; gap: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; align-items: flex-start;">' +
                                 '<div class="ach-icon" style="width: 20px; height: 20px; background: #eff6ff; border-radius: 50%; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center; color: #3b82f6; flex-shrink: 0; margin-top: 1px;">' + iconSvg + '</div>' +
                                 '<div class="ach-content" style="flex: 1;"><div class="desc" style="font-size: 8.5pt; color: #4b5563; line-height: 1.35;">' + lineHtml + (isLast ? linkHtml : '') + '</div></div>' +
                               '</div>';
                      }).join('');
                    }
                  }).join('')}
                  </div>
                ` : ""}

                ${state.skillLevels && state.skillLevels.length > 0 ? `
