                  <div class="section-title" style="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: 700; color: #71717a; text-transform: uppercase; border-bottom: 1px solid #e5e7eb; padding-bottom: 2pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; letter-spacing: 0.5px;">LANGUAGES</div>
                  <div style="margin-bottom: 12pt;">
                  ${state.skillLevels.map(s => {
                      let filledDots = Math.round(Number(s.level) / 20);
                      let dotsHtml = '';
                      for(let i=0; i<5; i++) {
                          dotsHtml += '<div class="dot ' + (i >= filledDots ? 'empty' : '') + '" style="width: 6px; height: 6px; border-radius: 50%; background: ' + (i >= filledDots ? '#e5e7eb' : '#3b82f6') + ';"></div>';
                      }
                      return '<div class="lang-item" style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; font-size: 8.5pt; margin-bottom: 4pt; align-items: center; color: #374151; font-weight: 500;">' +
                               '<span>' + esc(s.name) + '</span>' +
                               '<div class="dots" style="display: flex; gap: 3px;">' + dotsHtml + '</div>' +
                             '</div>';
                  }).join('')}
                  </div>
                ` : ""}

                ${certifications.length > 0 ? `
                  <div class="section-title" style="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: 700; color: #71717a; text-transform: uppercase; border-bottom: 1px solid #e5e7eb; padding-bottom: 2pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; letter-spacing: 0.5px;">CERTIFICATION</div>
                  <div style="margin-bottom: 12pt;">
                  ${certifications.map(c => {
                    if (!c.linkType) c.linkType = 'separate';
                    const nameHtml = applyTextLink(esc(c.name), c, false);
                    const sepLink = (!isTextLink(c) && c.link) ? ` <a href="${getUrl(c.link)}" class="pdf-link" target="_blank" style="color:inherit; text-decoration:none;">↗</a>` : '';
                    return `
                    <div class="item" style="margin-bottom: 8pt;">
                      <div class="item-title" style="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: 700; color: #1e3a8a;">
                        ${nameHtml}${sepLink}
                      </div>
                      <div class="desc" style="font-size: 8.5pt; color: #4b5563; line-height: 1.35; margin-top:2pt;">${esc(c.date)}</div>
                    </div>`;
                  }).join('')}
                  </div>
                ` : ""}

                ${extracurricular.length > 0 ? `
                  <div class="section-title" style="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: 700; color: #71717a; text-transform: uppercase; border-bottom: 1px solid #e5e7eb; padding-bottom: 2pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; letter-spacing: 0.5px;">EXTRACURRICULAR</div>
                  ${extracurricular.map(e => {
                    if (!e.linkType) e.linkType = 'separate';
                    const orgHtml = applyTextLink(esc(e.org), e, false);
                    const sepLink = (!isTextLink(e) && e.link) ? buildSeparateLink(e, false, e.linkText || 'Link') : '';
                    return `
                    <div class="item" style="margin-bottom: 8pt;">
                      <div class="item-title" style="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: 700; color: #1e3a8a;">${orgHtml}${sepLink} ${e.role ? `<span style="font-size: 9pt; color: #3b82f6; font-weight: 500;">- ${esc(e.role)}</span>` : ''}</div>
                      <div class="desc" style="font-size: 8.5pt; color: #4b5563; line-height: 1.35; margin-top:2pt;">${formatText(e.desc)}</div>
                    </div>`;
                  }).join('')}
                ` : ""}

                ${hobArr.length > 0 || langArr.length > 0 ? `
                  <div class="section-title" style="font-size: 10pt; font-weight: 700; color: #71717a; text-transform: uppercase; border-bottom: 1px solid #e5e7eb; padding-bottom: 2pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; letter-spacing: 0.5px;">INTERESTS</div>
                  <div class="desc" style="margin-bottom: 12pt; font-size: 8.5pt; color: #4b5563; line-height: 1.35;">
                    ${langArr.length > 0 ? `<div style="margin-bottom: 4pt;"><strong>Languages:</strong> ${langArr.join(', ')}</div>` : ''}
                    ${hobArr.length > 0 ? `<div><strong>Hobbies:</strong> ${hobArr.join(', ')}</div>` : ''}
                  </div>
               ` : ""}
              </div>
            </div>
          `;
        }
        })(previewState);
      }

      async function rewriteText(event, type, index = null) {
          const btn = event.currentTarget;
          let currentText = "";

          if (type === 'summary') currentText = state.summary;
          else if (type === 'experience') currentText = state.experience[index].desc;
          else if (type === 'projects') currentText = state.projects[index].desc;
          else if (type === 'extracurricular') currentText = state.extracurricular[index].desc;

          if (!currentText || currentText.trim() === "") {
              showToast("info","Write a Draft First","Add some text before enhancing with AI.");
              return;
          }

          const originalHTML = btn.innerHTML;
          btn.innerHTML = "⏳ Enhancing...";
          btn.disabled = true;

          try {
              const response = await fetch("/api/ai/rewrite", {
                  method: "POST",
                  headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
                  body: JSON.stringify({ 
                    text: currentText, 
                    context: type 
                  }),
              });

              if (!response.ok) throw new Error("Failed to connect to AI server.");

              const data = await response.json();
              const enhancedText = data.enhancedText || data.text || data.result;

             if (enhancedText) {
                  // Removed the broken isPristine variable to prevent crashes
                  if (type === 'summary') state.summary = enhancedText;
                  else if (type === 'experience') state.experience[index].desc = enhancedText;
                  else if (type === 'projects') state.projects[index].desc = enhancedText;
                  else if (type === 'extracurricular') state.extracurricular[index].desc = enhancedText;

                  // Make sure the AI enhanced text overrides the sample data
                  state._touched[type] = true; 

                  renderInputs();
                  render();
              }
          } catch (err) {
              console.error("AI Enhance Error:", err);
              showToast("error","Enhancement Failed","Make sure your server is running on port 5000.");
          } finally {
              btn.innerHTML = originalHTML;
              btn.disabled = false;
          }
      }

      async function saveResumeToDB() {
  const userId = localStorage.getItem("userId");
  const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
 const existingResumeId = urlParams.get("id") || urlParams.get("resumeId");
 
  // Validate using current template's data
  if (!state.name || !state.email) {
    showToast("warning", "Required Fields", "Name and Email are required to save.");
    return;
  }
 
  const payload = {
    userId: userId,
    resumeId: existingResumeId,
    personalInfo: {
      name: state.name,
      email: state.email,
      phone: state.phone,
    },
    templateType: currentTemplate,
    // Save the full per-template state map + which template is active
    templateSpecificInputs: {
      _perTemplateStates: templateStates,
      _activeTemplate: currentTemplate,
      // Also spread current template state at top level for backwards compat
      ...templateStates[currentTemplate],
      template: currentTemplate,
    },
  };
 
  try {
    const response = await fetch("/api/resume", {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      body: JSON.stringify(payload),
    });
 
    const result = await response.json();
 
    if (response.ok) {
      showToast("success", "Saved!", "Your resume has been saved successfully.");
      if (!existingResumeId && result.data && result.data._id) {
        window.history.replaceState(null, "", `/editor.html?id=${result.data._id}`);
      }
    } else {
      showToast("error", "Server Error", result.error || "Something went wrong.");
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Save error:", error);
    showToast("error", "Network Error", "Is your server running on port 5000?");
  }
}

      async function loadResumeData(id) {
  try {
    const response = await fetch(`/api/resume/${id}`);
    if (!response.ok) throw new Error("Failed to load");
 
    const data = await response.json();
 
    if (data && data.templateSpecificInputs) {
      const tsi = data.templateSpecificInputs;
 
     if (tsi._perTemplateStates) {
        // New format: restore each template's state
        TEMPLATES.forEach(t => {
          if (tsi._perTemplateStates[t]) {
            templateStates[t] = { ...freshTemplateState(), ...tsi._perTemplateStates[t] };
            // FIX: Force all fields to be "touched" so sample data is hidden immediately
            if (!templateStates[t]._touched) templateStates[t]._touched = {};
            Object.keys(SAMPLE_DATA).forEach(k => templateStates[t]._touched[k] = true);
          }
        });
        currentTemplate = tsi._activeTemplate || data.templateType || "academic";
      } else {
        // Legacy format: load data into the saved template only
        const savedTemplate = tsi.template || data.templateType || "academic";
        currentTemplate = savedTemplate;
        const legacyState = { ...tsi };
        delete legacyState.template;
        templateStates[savedTemplate] = { ...freshTemplateState(), ...legacyState };
        // FIX: Force all fields to be "touched" so sample data is hidden immediately
        if (!templateStates[savedTemplate]._touched) templateStates[savedTemplate]._touched = {};
        Object.keys(SAMPLE_DATA).forEach(k => templateStates[savedTemplate]._touched[k] = true);
      }
 
      // Update UI to reflect loaded template
     const templateLabels = {
        academic: 'Technical Executive', minimal: 'Sleek Minimalist',
        modern: 'Contemporary Creative', attorney: 'Traditional Corporate',
        innovative: 'Executive Innovative', bordered: 'Bordered Academic'
      };
      const trigger = document.getElementById('template-select-trigger');
      const menu = document.getElementById('template-select-menu');
      if (trigger) trigger.textContent = templateLabels[currentTemplate] || currentTemplate;
      if (menu) {
        menu.querySelectorAll('.custom-select-option').forEach(o => {
          o.classList.toggle('selected', o.dataset.value === currentTemplate);
        });
      }
 
      updateTemplate(currentTemplate);
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Error loading resume:", error);
    showToast("error", "Load Failed", "Could not load your saved resume data.");
  }
}
 

      window.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", async () => {
        const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
        const requestedTemplate = urlParams.get("template");
        const resumeId = urlParams.get("id") || urlParams.get("resumeId");

        if (resumeId) {
  loadResumeData(resumeId);
} else if (requestedTemplate) {
  const _labels2 = {
    academic: 'Technical Executive', minimal: 'Sleek Minimalist',
    modern: 'Contemporary Creative', attorney: 'Traditional Corporate',
    innovative: 'Executive Innovative', bordered: 'Bordered Academic'
  };
  const _tr2 = document.getElementById('template-select-trigger');
  const _mn2 = document.getElementById('template-select-menu');
  if (_tr2) _tr2.textContent = _labels2[requestedTemplate] || requestedTemplate;
  if (_mn2) _mn2.querySelectorAll('.custom-select-option').forEach(o => {
    o.classList.toggle('selected', o.dataset.value === requestedTemplate);
  });
  currentTemplate = requestedTemplate;
  updateTemplate(requestedTemplate);

  if (urlParams.get('autoStudio') === '1') {
    await document.fonts.ready;
    await convertToStudio();
  }
} else {
  updateTemplate("academic");
}
      });

      /**
 * DROP-IN REPLACEMENT for convertToStudio() in editor.html
 *
 * Changes vs. old version
 * ───────────────────────
 * 1. Removes transform BEFORE any getBoundingClientRect() calls, then waits
 *    two requestAnimationFrame callbacks so the browser fully reflows.
 *    → every coordinate is now in the page's natural pixel space.
 *
 * 2. Single incrementing Z-counter for ALL items (bg shapes, borders, text).
 *    DOM traversal is depth-first, so parents always get lower z-index than
 *    their children — exactly matching CSS stacking behaviour.
 *
 * 3. Backgrounds + all 4 border sides are captured as thin shape elements.
 *
 * 4. SVG icons are serialised with outerHTML into an inline text-element div
 *    so they render identically in the Studio canvas.
 *
 * 5. CSS ::before / ::after pseudo-content is captured:
 *    – non-positioned  → inlined into the text element HTML
 *    – absolutely positioned (e.g. list dashes "–") → a separate sibling element
 *
 * 6. Padding is preserved on text elements (keeps list indentation).
 *
 * 7. Text elements have NO fixed height — they expand naturally to their content.
 *
 * HOW TO APPLY
 * ─────────────
 * In editor.html find:
 *
 *   async function convertToStudio() {
 *
 * …and replace the entire function (up to and including its closing `}`)
 * with the function below.
 */

      /**
 * DROP-IN REPLACEMENT for convertToStudio() in editor.html  (v2 — alignment fix)
 *
 * HOW TO APPLY
 * ─────────────
 * In editor.html, find:   async function convertToStudio() {
 * Select the entire function down to its closing brace } and replace with this.
 *
 * WHAT WAS WRONG
 * ──────────────
 * 1. w + 15 added to every text element width regardless of text-align.
 *    Right-aligned text (dates, locations) → appeared 15 px too far LEFT.
 *    Center-aligned text → appeared shifted by 7.5 px.
 * 2. white-space was always forced to "pre-wrap", overriding "nowrap" on date/
 *    contact spans → those elements incorrectly wrapped onto a second line.
 * 3. line-height was stored as absolute px, causing font-size mismatch drift.
 */

      async function convertToStudio(callerBtn) {
          if (!localStorage.getItem("userId")) return showToast("info","Login Required","Please log in to use the Customizer Studio.");

          const preview = document.getElementById("preview");
          const btn = callerBtn || document.createElement('button');
          const origHTML = btn.innerHTML || '';
          if (btn.isConnected) { btn.innerHTML = "&#x23F3; Exporting..."; btn.disabled = true; }

          /* ── Strip transform so getBoundingClientRect returns natural px ── */
          preview.classList.remove("animating");
          const origTransform  = preview.style.transform;
          const origTransition = preview.style.transition;
          const origMarginB    = preview.style.marginBottom;
          preview.style.transform    = "none";
          preview.style.transition   = "none";
          preview.style.marginBottom = "0";

          /* Two rAF callbacks — browser fully reflows before we measure */
          await new Promise(r => requestAnimationFrame(() => requestAnimationFrame(r)));

          const PR    = preview.getBoundingClientRect();
          const pageH = preview.offsetHeight;

          /* ── Config ── */
          const SKIP_TAGS = new Set(["script","style","head","noscript","meta","link","title"]);
          const SVG_KIDS  = new Set(["path","circle","rect","line","polygon","ellipse",
                                     "defs","use","g","mask","clippath","stop",
                                     "radialgradient","lineargradient","symbol","animate",
                                     "filter","feblend","feflood","fecomposite","feoffset",
                                     "femorphology","fecolormatrix","femerge","femergenode",
                                     "feturbulence","fecomponenttransfer",
                                     "fefuncr","fefuncg","fefuncb","fefunca"]);
          const BLOCK_D   = new Set(["block","flex","grid","table","table-cell","table-row",
                                     "list-item","inline-flex","inline-grid","table-row-group",
                                     "table-header-group","table-footer-group",
                                     "table-column","table-column-group"]);

          let Z = 1;
          const items = [];

          /* ── Helpers ── */
          const getR = node => {
              const r = node.getBoundingClientRect();
              return {
                  l: +(r.left - PR.left).toFixed(1),
                  t: +(r.top  - PR.top ).toFixed(1),
                  w: +r.width .toFixed(1),
                  h: +r.height.toFixed(1)
              };
          };

          /*
           * KEY FIX 1 — alignment-aware width
           * Right/center aligned text must NOT get extra width or it shifts left.
           * Left-aligned gets only +2 px (minimal anti-clip buffer).
           */
          const safeWidth = (measuredW, align) => {
              if (align === "right" || align === "end")  return measuredW;
              if (align === "center")                     return measuredW;
              return measuredW + 2;
          };

          /*
           * KEY FIX 2 — unitless line-height ratio
           * Avoids drift when font sizes differ between editor and Studio canvas.
           */
          const lhRatio = s => {
              const lh = parseFloat(s.lineHeight);
              const fs = parseFloat(s.fontSize);
              if (!isFinite(lh) || !isFinite(fs) || fs === 0) return "1.4";
              return (lh / fs).toFixed(3);
          };

          const pseudoText = (node, ps) => {
              try {
                  const s = window.getComputedStyle(node, ps);
                  const c = s.content;
                  if (!c || ["none","normal","auto",'""',"''"].includes(c)) return "";
                  return c.replace(/^["']|["']$/g, "")
                          .replace(/\\A/g, "\n")
                          .replace(/\\25CF/g, "\u2022");
              } catch(e) { return ""; }
          };

          const hasBlockChild = node => {
              for (const c of node.childNodes) {
                  if (c.nodeType !== 1) continue;
                  const ct = c.tagName.toLowerCase();
                  if (SKIP_TAGS.has(ct) || SVG_KIDS.has(ct) || ct === "svg") continue;
                  if (BLOCK_D.has(window.getComputedStyle(c).display)) return true;
              }
              return false;
          };

          /* ── Main DOM walker (depth-first) ── */
          function walk(node) {
              if (node.nodeType !== 1) return;

              const tag = node.tagName.toLowerCase();
              if (SKIP_TAGS.has(tag) || SVG_KIDS.has(tag)) return;

              if (node === preview) { node.childNodes.forEach(c => walk(c)); return; }

              const s = window.getComputedStyle(node);
              if (s.display === "none" || s.visibility === "hidden") return;

              const { l, t, w, h } = getR(node);
              if (w < 0.5 || h < 0.5) return;

              /* <img> */
              if (tag === "img") {
                  items.push({ k:"img", l, t, w, h, z:Z++, src:node.src, br:s.borderRadius });
                  return;
              }

              /* <svg> → inline block (preserves icons exactly) */
              if (tag === "svg") {
                  items.push({ k:"svg", l, t, w, h, z:Z++, html:node.outerHTML, color:s.color });
                  return;
              }

              /* Background colour / image */
              const bgC = s.backgroundColor, bgI = s.backgroundImage;
              const hasBgC = bgC && bgC !== "rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)";
              const hasBgI = bgI && bgI !== "none";
              if (hasBgC || hasBgI) {
                  let st = "";
                  if (hasBgC) st += `background-color:${bgC};`;
                  if (hasBgI) st += `background-image:${bgI};background-size:${s.backgroundSize};background-position:${s.backgroundPosition};background-repeat:${s.backgroundRepeat};`;
                  if (s.borderRadius !== "0px") st += `border-radius:${s.borderRadius};`;
                  if (s.opacity !== "1")        st += `opacity:${s.opacity};`;
                  items.push({ k:"shape", l, t, w, h, z:Z++, st });
              }

              /* All 4 border sides → thin shape elements */
              for (const [side, isHoriz] of [["Top",1],["Bottom",1],["Left",0],["Right",0]]) {
                  const bpx = parseFloat(s[`border${side}Width`]);
                  const bst = s[`border${side}Style`];
                  const bc  = s[`border${side}Color`];
                  if (bpx > 0.1 && bst !== "none" && bc !== "rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)") {
                      items.push({ k:"shape",
                          l: side === "Right"  ? l+w-bpx : l,
                          t: side === "Bottom" ? t+h-bpx : t,
                          w: isHoriz ? w   : bpx,
                          h: isHoriz ? bpx : h,
                          z: Z++, st: `background-color:${bc};`
                      });
                  }
              }

              /* Text leaf */
              const hasText = (node.innerText || "").trim().length > 0;
              if (!hasBlockChild(node) && hasText) {

                  const bs   = window.getComputedStyle(node, "::before");
                  const as_  = window.getComputedStyle(node, "::after");
                  const bTxt = pseudoText(node, "::before");
                  const aTxt = pseudoText(node, "::after");

                  let html = node.innerHTML;

                  /* Non-positioned pseudo-elements: inline them */
                  if (bTxt && bs.position  !== "absolute" && bs.position  !== "fixed")
                      html = `<span>${bTxt}</span>` + html;
                  if (aTxt && as_.position !== "absolute" && as_.position !== "fixed")
                      html += `<span>${aTxt}</span>`;

                  /* Absolutely-positioned ::before (list "–" dashes etc.) */
                  if (bTxt && (bs.position === "absolute" || bs.position === "fixed")) {
                      items.push({ k:"text",
                          l: l + (parseFloat(bs.left) || 0),
                          t: t + (parseFloat(bs.top)  || 0),
                          w: 20, z:Z++, html: bTxt,
                          st: `font-family:${s.fontFamily.replace(/"/g,"'")};font-size:${s.fontSize};font-weight:${bs.fontWeight||s.fontWeight};color:${bs.color||s.color};line-height:${lhRatio(s)};white-space:pre;overflow:visible;`
                      });
                  }

                  /* Preserve padding (keeps list indentation) */
                  const pl  = parseFloat(s.paddingLeft)   || 0;
                  const pt2 = parseFloat(s.paddingTop)    || 0;
                  const pr2 = parseFloat(s.paddingRight)  || 0;
                  const pb2 = parseFloat(s.paddingBottom) || 0;
                  const padSt = (pl||pt2||pr2||pb2)
                      ? `padding:${pt2}px ${pr2}px ${pb2}px ${pl}px;` : "";

                  const ff    = s.fontFamily.replace(/"/g,"'");
                  const ls    = s.letterSpacing === "normal" ? "0px" : s.letterSpacing;
                  const fv    = (s.fontVariant && s.fontVariant !== "normal")
                                ? `font-variant:${s.fontVariant};` : "";
                  const td    = (s.textDecoration && s.textDecoration !== "none")
                                ? `text-decoration:${s.textDecoration};` : "";
                  const align = s.textAlign;

                  /* KEY FIX 1: alignment-aware width */
                  const tw = safeWidth(w, align);

                  /* KEY FIX 2: preserve white-space (don't override nowrap) */
                  const ws = s.whiteSpace || "normal";

                  items.push({ k:"text", l, t, w:tw, z:Z++, html,
                      st: `font-family:${ff};font-size:${s.fontSize};font-weight:${s.fontWeight};font-style:${s.fontStyle};color:${s.color};text-align:${align};line-height:${lhRatio(s)};letter-spacing:${ls};text-transform:${s.textTransform};${td}${fv}${padSt}white-space:${ws};overflow:visible;`
                  });
                  return;
              }

              node.childNodes.forEach(c => walk(c));
          }

          walk(preview);

          /* ── Serialise → HTML string ── */
          let htmlStr = "";
          for (const it of items) {
              const base = `position:absolute;left:${it.l}px;top:${it.t}px;width:${it.w}px;height:${it.h}px;z-index:${it.z};`;
              if (it.k === "shape") {
                  htmlStr += `<div class="element shape-element" style="${base}${it.st}"></div>\n`;
              } else if (it.k === "text") {
                  /* No fixed height — expands naturally to content */
                  htmlStr += `<div class="element text-element" contenteditable="false" spellcheck="false" style="position:absolute;left:${it.l}px;top:${it.t}px;width:${it.w}px;z-index:${it.z};${it.st}">${it.html}</div>\n`;
              } else if (it.k === "img") {
                  const br = (it.br && it.br !== "0px") ? `border-radius:${it.br};` : "";
                  htmlStr += `<div class="element image-element" style="${base}background-image:url('${it.src}');background-size:cover;background-position:center;${br}"></div>\n`;
              } else if (it.k === "svg") {
                  htmlStr += `<div class="element text-element" contenteditable="false" spellcheck="false" style="position:absolute;left:${it.l}px;top:${it.t}px;width:${it.w}px;height:${it.h}px;z-index:${it.z};display:flex;align-items:center;color:${it.color};">${it.html}</div>\n`;
              }
          }

          /* ── Restore ── */
          preview.style.transform    = origTransform;
          preview.style.transition   = origTransition;
          preview.style.marginBottom = origMarginB;

          btn.innerHTML = origHTML;
          btn.disabled  = false;

          try {
              localStorage.setItem("tempStudioHtml",   htmlStr);
              localStorage.setItem("tempStudioHeight", String(pageH));
              window.location.href = "customize.html?mode=temp";
          } catch(e) {
              console.error(e);
              showToast("error", "Export Failed", "Could not serialize resume. Try reducing content.");
          }
      }

      /* ── Mobile Preview Toggle ── */
function toggleMobilePreview() {
  const previewWrap = document.getElementById('preview-wrap');
  const btn = document.getElementById('mobile-preview-btn');
  const isVisible = previewWrap.classList.toggle('mobile-visible');

  btn.innerHTML = isVisible
    ? `<svg width="13" height="13" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><line x1="18" y1="6" x2="6" y2="18"/><line x1="6" y1="6" x2="18" y2="18"/></svg> Close`
    : `<svg width="13" height="13" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><rect x="2" y="3" width="20" height="14" rx="2"/><line x1="8" y1="21" x2="16" y2="21"/><line x1="12" y1="17" x2="12" y2="21"/></svg> Preview`;
}
    </script>
  </body>
</html>
